          ādarśakārādibhis tīrthakarair nirūpitam/ 
 [l. 6.78] 
 cittadvāreṇātmeśvarasaṃbandhahetur yogaḥ/ sa ca dvividhaḥ kriyālakṣaṇaḥ
          kriyoparamalakṣaṇaś ceti/ tatra japadhyānādirūpaḥ kriyālakṣaṇaḥ/ kriyoparamalakṣaṇas tu
          niṣṭhāsaṃvidgatyādisaṃjñitaḥ/ 
 [l. 6.81] 
 dharmārthasādhakavyāpāro vidhiḥ/ sa ca dvividhaḥ — pradhānabhūto guṇabhūtaś ca/ tatra
          pradhānabhūtaḥ sākṣād dharmahetuś caryā/ sā dvividhā vrataṃ dvārāṇi ceti/ tatra
          bhasmasnānaśayanopahārajapapradakṣiṇāni vratam/ tad uktam bhagavatā nakulīśena — bhasmanā
          triṣavaṇaṃ snāyīta bhasmani śayīteti/ 
 atropahāro niyamaḥ/ sa ca ṣaḍaṅgaḥ/ tad uktaṃ sūtrakāreṇa —
          hasitagītanṛtyahuḍukkāranamaskārajapyaṣaḍaṅgopahāreṇopatiṣṭheteti/ tatra hasitaṃ nāma
          kaṇṭhoṣṭhapuṭavisphūrjanapuraḥsaram ahahety aṭṭahāsaḥ/ 
 gītaṃ gāndharvaśāstrasamayānusāreṇa maheśvarasaṃbandhiguṇadharmādinimittānāṃ cintanam/
          nṛtyam api nāṭyaśāstrānusāreṇa hastapādādīnām utkṣepaṇādikam aṅgapratyaṅgopāṅgasahitaṃ
          bhāvābhāvasametaṃ ca prayoktavyam/ huḍukkāro nāma jihvātālusaṃyogān niṣpādyamānaḥ puṇyo
          vṛṣanādasadṛśo nādaḥ/ huḍug iti śabdānukāro vaṣaḍ itivat/ yatra laukikā bhavanti tatraitat
          sarvaṃ gūḍhaṃ prayoktavyam/ śiṣṭaṃ prasiddham/ dvārāṇi tu
          krāthanaspandanamandanaśṛṅgāraṇāvitatkaraṇāvitadbhāṣaṇāni/ tatrāsuptasyaiva
          suptaliṅgapradarśanaṃ krāthanam/ vāyvabhibhūtasyeva śarīrāvayavānāṃ kampanaṃ spandanam/
          upahatapādendriyasyeva gamanaṃ mandanam/ rūpayauvanasaṃpannāṃ kāminīm avalokyātmānaṃ
          kāmukam iva yair vilāsaiḥ pradarśayati tac chṛṅgāraṇam/ kāryākāryavivekavikalasyeva
          lokaninditakarmakaraṇam avitatkaraṇam/ vyāhatāpārthakādiśabdoccāraṇam avitadbhāṣaṇam iti/
          guṇabhūtas tu vidhiś caryānugrāhako ’nusnānādir
          bhaikṣyocchiṣṭādinirmitāyogyatāpratyayanivṛttyarthaḥ/ tad apy uktaṃ sūtrakāreṇa —
          anusnānanirmālyaliṅgadhārīti/ 
 [l. 6.101] 
 tatra samāso nāma dharmimātrābhidhānam/ tac ca prathamasūtra eva kṛtam/ pañcānāṃ
          padārthānāṃ pramāṇataḥ pañcābhidhānaṃ vistaraḥ/ sa khalu rāśīkarabhāṣye draṣṭavyaḥ/ eteṣāṃ
          yathāsaṃbhavaṃ lakṣaṇato ’saṃkareṇābhidhānaṃ vibhāgaḥ/ sa tu vihita eva/ śāstrāntarebhyo
          ’mīṣāṃ guṇātiśayena kathanaṃ viśeṣaḥ/ tathā hi — anyatra duḥkhanivṛttir eva duḥkhāntaḥ/
          iha tu pāramaiśvaryaprāptiś ca/ anyatrābhūtvā bhāvi kāryam/ iha tu nityaṃ paśvādi/ anyatra
          sāpekṣaṃ kāraṇam/ iha tu nirapekṣo bhagavān eva/ anyatra kaivalyādiphalako yogaḥ/ iha tu
          pāramaiśvaryaduḥkhāntaphalakaḥ/ anyatra punar āvṛttirūpasvargādiphalako vidhiḥ/ iha punar
          apunarāvṛttirūpasāmīpyādiphalakaḥ/ 
 [l. 6.110] 
 nanu mahad etad indrajālaṃ yan nirapekṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti/ tathātve
          karmavaiphalyaṃ sarvakāryāṇāṃ samasamayasamutpādaś ceti doṣadvayaṃ prāduḥṣyāt/ 
 [l. 6.112] 
 maivaṃ manyethāḥ/ vyadhikaraṇatvāt/ 
 yadi nirapekṣasya bhagavataḥ kāraṇatvaṃ syāt tarhi karmaṇo vaiphalye kim āyātam/
          prayojanābhāva iti cet — kasya prayojanābhāvaḥ karmavaiphalye kāraṇam/ kiṃ karmiṇaḥ kiṃ vā
          bhagavataḥ/ nādyaḥ/ īśvarecchānugṛhītasya karmaṇaḥ saphalatvopapatteḥ/ tadananugṛhītasya
          yayātiprabhṛtikarmavat kadācin niṣphalatvasaṃbhavāc ca/ na caitāvatā karmasv apravṛttiḥ/
          karṣakādivad upapatteḥ/ īśvarecchāyattatvāc ca paśūnāṃ pravṛtteḥ/ nāpi dvitīyaḥ/
          parameśvarasya paryāptakāmatvena karmasādhyaprayojanāpekṣāyā abhāvāt/ yad uktaṃ
          samasamayasamutpāda iti tad apy ayuktam/ acintyaśaktikasya parameśvarasyecchānuvidhāyinyā
          avyāhatakriyāśaktyā kāryakāritvābhyupagamāt/ tad uktaṃ saṃpradāyavidbhiḥ — 
 [l. 6.122] 
 
 karmādinirapekṣas tu svecchācārī yato hy ayam/ 
 tataḥ kāraṇataḥ śāstre sarvakāraṇakāraṇam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 6.124] 
 nanu darśanāntare ’pīśvarajñānān mokṣo labhyata eveti kuto ’sya viśeṣa iti cet — maivaṃ
          vādīḥ/ vikalpānupapatteḥ/ kim īśvaraviṣayajñānamātraṃ nirvāṇakāraṇaṃ kiṃ vā sākṣātkāraḥ
          atha vā yathāvat tattvaniścayaḥ/ nādyaḥ/ śāstram antareṇāpi prākṛtajanavad devānām adhipo
          mahādeva iti jñānotpattimātreṇa mokṣasiddhau śāstrābhyāsavaiphalyaprasaṅgāt/ nāpi
          dvitīyaḥ/ anekamalapracayopacitānāṃ piśitalocanānāṃ paśūnāṃ
          parameśvarasākṣātkārānupapatteḥ/ tṛtīye ’smanmatāpātaḥ/ pāśupataśāstram antareṇa yathāvat
          tattvaniścayānupapatteḥ/ tad uktam ācāryaiḥ — 
 
 jñānamātre vṛthā śāstraṃ sākṣāddṛṣṭis tu durlabhā/ 
 pañcārthād anyato nāsti yathāvat tattvaniścayaḥ// iti/ 
 
 tasmāt puruṣārthakāmaiḥ puruṣadhaureyaiḥ pañcārthapratipādanaparaṃ pāśupataśāstram
          āśrayaṇīyam iti ramaṇīyam// 
 iti sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe nakulīśapāśupatadarśanam// 
 
 
 atha śaivadarśanam 
 [l. 7.1] 
 tam imaṃ parameśvaraḥ karmādinirapekṣaḥ kāraṇam iti pakṣaṃ
          vaiṣamyanaighṛṇyadoṣadūṣitatvāt pratikṣipantaḥ kecana māheśvarāḥ śaivāgamasiddhāntatattvaṃ
          yathāvad īkṣamāṇāḥ karmādisāpekṣaḥ parameśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti pakṣaṃ kaṣīkurvāṇāḥ
          pakṣāntaram upakṣipanti patipaśupāśabhedāt trayaḥ padārthā iti/ 
 [l. 7.5] 
 tad uktaṃ tantratattvajñaiḥ — 
 
 tripadārthaṃ catuṣpādaṃ mahātantraṃ jagadguruḥ/ 
 sūtreṇaikena saṃkṣipya prāha vistarataḥ punaḥ// iti/ 
 
 asyārthaḥ/ uktās trayaḥ padārthā yasmin santi tat tripadārthaṃ vidyākriyāyogacaryākhāś
          catvāraḥ pādā yasmiṃs tac catuścaraṇaṃ mahātantram iti/ tatra paśūnām asvatantratvāt
          pāśānām acaitanyāt tadvilakṣaṇasya patyuḥ prathamam uddeśaḥ/ cetanatvasādharmyāt paśūnāṃ
          tadānantaryam/ avaśiṣṭānāṃ pāśānām ante viniveśa iti kramaniyamaḥ/ dīkṣāyāḥ
          paramapuruṣārthahetutvāt tasyāś ca paśupāśeśvarasvarūpanirṇayopāyabhūtena
          mantramantreśvarādimāhātmyaniścāyakena jñānena vinā niṣpādayitum aśakyatvāt
          tadavabodhakasya vidyāpādasya prāthamyam/ anekavidhasāṅgadīkṣāvidhipradarśakasya
          kriyāpādasya tadānantaryam/ yogena vinā nābhimataprāptir iti sāṅgayogajñāpakasya
          yogapādasya taduttaratvam/ vihitācaraṇaniṣiddhavarjanarūpāṃ caryāṃ vinā yogo ’pi na
          nirvahatīti tatpratipādakasya caryāpādasya caramatvam iti vivekaḥ/ 
 [l. 7.20] 
 tatra patipadārthaḥ śivo ’bhimataḥ/ muktātmanāṃ vidyeśvarādīnāṃ ca yady api śivatvam asti
          tathāpi parameśvarapāratantryāt svātantryaṃ nāsti/ tataś ca tanukaraṇabhuvanādīnāṃ
          bhāvānāṃ saṃniveśaviśiṣṭatvena kāryatvam avagamyate/ tena ca kāryatvenaiṣāṃ
          buddhimatpūrvakatvam anumīyata ity anumānavaśāt parameśvaraprasiddhir upapadyate/ 
 [l. 7.25] 
 nanu dehasyaiva tāvat kāryatvam asiddham/ na hi kvacit kenacit kadācid dehaḥ kriyamāṇo
          dṛṣṭacaraḥ/ satyam/ tathāpi na kenacit kriyamāṇatvaṃ dehasya dṛṣṭam iti
          kartṛdarśanāpahnavo na yujyate/ tasyānumeyatvenāpy upapatteḥ/ tathā hi/ dehādikaṃ kāryaṃ
          bhavitum arhati saṃniveśaviśiṣṭatvād vinaśvaratvād vā ghaṭādivat/ tena ca kāryatvena
          buddhimatpūrvakatvam anumātuṃ sukaram eva/ vimataṃ sakartṛkaṃ kāryatvād ghaṭavat/ yad

 [l. 7.49]

 yo yaj jānāti kurute sa tad eveti susthitam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 7.53] 
 astu tarhi svatantra īśvaraḥ kartā/ sa tu nāśarīraḥ/ ghaṭādikāryasya śarīravatā
          kulālādinā kriyamāṇatvadarśanāt/ śarīravattve cāsmadādivad īśvaraḥ kleśayukto ’sarvajñaḥ
          parimitaśaktiṃ prāpnuyād iti cet — maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ/ aśarīrasyāpy ātmanaḥ
          svaśarīraspandādau kartṛtvadarśanāt/ abhyupagamyāpi brūmahe/ śarīravattve ’pi bhagavato na
          prāguktadoṣānuṣaṅgaḥ/ parameśvarasya hi malakarmādipāśajālāsaṃbhavena prākṛtaṃ śarīraṃ na

 [l. 7.86]

 [l. 7.105] 
 paśus trividhaḥ/ vijñānākalapralayākalasakalabhedāt/ tatra prathamo vijñānayogasaṃnyāsair

 tatra prathamo dviprakāro bhavati samāptakaluṣāsamāptakaluṣabhedāt/ tatrādyān

          prāpayati/ tad vidyeśvarāṣṭakaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ bahudaivatye —

 ekanetras tathaivaikarudraś cāpi trimūrtikaḥ//

 [l. 7.118]

          —

 malayuktas tatrādyo malakarmayuto dvitīyaḥ syāt// 
 malamāyākarmayutaḥ sakalas teṣu dvidhā bhaved ādyaḥ/ 
 ādyaḥ samāptakaluṣo ’samāptakaluṣo dvitīyaḥ syāt//

 mantrāṃś ca karoty aparāṃs te coktāḥ koṭayaḥ sapta// iti/

 [l. 7.136] 
 puryaṣṭakam api tatraiva nirdiṣṭam — 
 
 syāt puryaṣṭakam antaḥkaraṇaṃ dhīkarma karaṇāni/ iti/ 
 
 [l. 7.138] 
 vivṛtaṃ cāghoraśivācāryeṇa — puryaṣṭakaṃ nāma pratipuruṣaṃ niyataḥ sargād ārabhya
          kalpāntaṃ mokṣāntaṃ vā sthitaḥ pṛthivyādikalāparyantas triṃśattattvātmakaḥ sūkṣmo dehaḥ/
          tathā coktaṃ tattvasaṃgrahe — 
 
 vasudhādyas tattvagaṇaḥ pratipuṃniyataḥ kalānto ’yam/ 
 paryaṭati karmavaśād bhuvanajadeheṣv ayaṃ ca sarveṣu// iti/ 
 
 tathā cāyam arthaḥ samapadyata — antaḥkaraṇaśabdena manobuddhyahaṃkāravācinānyāny api
          puṃso bhogakriyāyām antaraṅgāṇi kalākālaniyatividyārāgaprakṛtiguṇākhyāni sapta tattvāny
          upalakṣyante/ dhīkarmaśabdena jñeyāni pañca bhūtāni tatkāraṇāni ca tanmātrāṇi vivakṣyante/
          karaṇaśabdena jñānakarmendriyadaśakaṃ saṃgṛhyate/ nanu śrīmatkālottare — 
 
 śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaś ca pañcakam/ 
 buddhir manas tv ahaṃkāraḥ puryaṣṭakam udāhṛtam// 
 
 iti śrūyate/ tat katham anyathā kathyate/ addhā/ ata eva ca tatrabhavatā rāmakaṇṭhena 
 rāmakaṇṭhena  ] ASS v.l., IV, Torella;  rāmakāṇḍena  A. 
  tat sūtraṃ triṃśattattvaparatayā vyākhyāyīty alam atiprapañcena/ 
 [l. 7.152] 
 tathāpi kathaṃ punar asya puryaṣṭakatvam/
          bhūtatanmātrabuddhīndriyakarmendriyāntaḥkaraṇasaṃjñaiḥ pañcabhir vargais tatkāraṇena
          guṇatattvena tadāpūrakeṇa pradhānena kalādipañcakātmanā vargeṇa cārabdhatvād ity
          avirodhaḥ/ tatra puryaṣṭakayutān viśiṣṭapuṇyasaṃpannān kāṃścid anugṛhya bhuvanapatitvam
          atra maheśvaro ’nantaḥ prayacchati/ tad uktam — 
 
 kāṃścid anugṛhya vitarati bhuvanapatitvaṃ maheśvaras teṣām/ iti/ 
 
 [l. 7.158] 
 sakalo ’pi dvividhaḥ/ pakvakaluṣāpakvakaluṣabhedāt/ tatrādyān parameśvaras
          tatparipākaparipāṭyā tadanuguṇaśaktipātena maṇḍalyādyaṣṭādaśottaraśatamantreśvarapadaṃ
          prāpayati/ tad uktam — 
 
 śeṣā bhavanti sakalāḥ kalādiyogād aharmukhe kāle/ 
 śatam aṣṭādaśa teṣāṃ kurute svayam eva mantreśān// 
 tatrāṣṭau maṇḍalinaḥ krodhādyās tatsamāś ca vīreśaḥ/ 
 śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śatarudrāḥ śatam ity aṣṭādaśābhyadhikam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 7.165] 
 tatparipākādhikyānurodhena śaktyupasaṃhāreṇa dīkṣākaraṇena mokṣaprado bhavaty

 [l. 7.169]

 [l. 7.171] 
 vyākṛtaṃ ca nārāyaṇkaṇṭhena/ tat sarvaṃ tata evāvadhāryam/ asmābhis tu vistarabhiyā na
          prastūyate/ apakvakaluṣān baddhān aṇūn bhogabhājo vidhatte parameśvaraḥ karmavaśāt/ tad
          apy uktam — 
 
 baddhāñ śeṣān aparān viniyuṅkte bhogabhuktaye puṃsaḥ/ 
 tatkarmaṇām anugamād ity evaṃ kīrtitāḥ paśavaḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 7.176] 
 atha pāśapadārthaḥ kathyate/ pāśaś caturvidhaḥ/ malakarmamāyārodhaśaktibhedāt/ nanu — 
 
 śaivāgameṣu mukhyaṃ patipaśupāśā iti kramāt tritayam/ 
 tatra patiḥ śiva uktaḥ paśavo hy aṇavo ’rthapañcakaṃ pāśāḥ// 
 
 iti pāśaḥ pañcavidhaḥ kathyate/ tat kathaṃ caturvidha iti gaṇyate/ ucyate — bindor
          māyātmanaḥ śivatattvapadavedanīyasya śivapadaprāptilakṣaṇaparamamuktyapekṣayā pāśatve ’pi
          tadyogasya vidyeśvarādipadaprāptihetutvenāparamuktitvāt pāśatvenānupādānam ity avirodhaḥ/
          ata evoktaṃ tattvaprakāśe — pāśāś caturvidhāḥ syur iti/ śrīmanmṛgendre ’pi — 
 
 prāvṛtīśo balaṃ karma māyākāryaṃ caturvidham/ 
 pāśajālaṃ samāsena dharmā nāmnaiva kīrtitāḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 7.187] 
 asyārthaḥ — prāvṛṇoti prakarṣeṇācchādayaty ātmanaḥ svābhāvikyau dṛkkriye iti prāvṛtir

 [l. 7.204]

 [l. 8.17] 
 kathaṃcid iti/ parameśvarābhinnagurucaraṇāravindayugalasamārādhanena
          parameśvaraghaṭitenaivety arthaḥ/ āsādyeti/ ā samantāt paripūrṇatayā sādayitvā
          svātmopabhogyatāṃ nirargalāṃ gamayitvā/ tad anena viditavedyatvena parārthaśāstrakaraṇe
          ’dhikāro darśitaḥ/ anyathā pratāraṇam eva prasajyeta/ māyottīrṇā api mahāmāyādhikṛtā

          anavacchinnaprakāśānandasvātantryaparamārtho maheśvaraḥ/tasya dāsyam/ dīyate ’smai svāminā
          sarvaṃ yathābhilaṣitam iti dāsaḥ/ parameśvarasvarūpasvātantryapātram ity arthaḥ/
          janaśabdenādhikāriviṣayaniyamābhāvaḥ prādarśi/ yasya yasya hīdaṃ svarūpakathanaṃ tasya
          tasya mahāphalaṃ bhavati/ prajñānasyaiva paramārthaphalatvāt/ tathopadiṣṭaṃ śivadṛṣṭau
          paramagurubhir bhagavatsomānandanāthapādaiḥ —

 jñāte śivatve sarvasthe pratipattyā dṛḍhātmanā// 
 karaṇena nāsti kṛtyaṃ kvāpi bhāvanayāpi vā/

 [l. 8.32] 
 apiśabdena svātmanas tadabhinnatām āviṣkurvatā pūrṇatvena svātmani
          parārthasaṃpattyatiriktaprayojanāntarāvakāśaś ca parākṛtaḥ/ parārthaś ca prayojanaṃ
          bhavaty eva/ tallakṣaṇayogāt/ na hy ayaṃ devaśāpaḥ svārtha eva prayojanaṃ na parārtha iti/
          ata evoktam akṣapādena — yam artham adhikṛtya pravartate tat prayojanam iti/ upaśabdaḥ
          sāmīpyārthaḥ/ tena janasya parameśvarasamīpatākaraṇamātraṃ phalam/ ata evāha — samasteti/
          parameśvaratālābhe hi sarvāḥ saṃpadas tanniṣyandamayyaḥ saṃpannā eva rohaṇācalalābhe

          kācana kāminī madanavihvalā virahakleśam asahamānā madanalekhāvalambanena
          svāvasthānivedanāni vidhatte/ tathā vegāt tannikaṭam aṭaty 
 ° aṭaty° ]  ASS v.l., IV; ° aṭanty°  A. 
  api tasminn avalokite ’pi tadavalokanaṃ tadīyaguṇaparāmarśābhāve janasādhāraṇatvaṃ
          prāpte hṛdayaṃgamabhāvaṃ na labhate/ yadā tu dūtīvacanāt tadīyaguṇaparāmarśaṃ karoti tadā
          tatkṣaṇam eva pūrṇabhāvam abhyeti/ evaṃ svātmani viśveśvarātmanā bhāsamāne ’pi
          tannirbhāsanaṃ tadīyaguṇaparāmarśavirahasamaye pūrṇabhāvaṃ na saṃpādayati/ 
 yadā tu guruvacanādinā sarvajñatvasarvakartṛtvādilakṣaṇaparameśvarotkarṣaparāmarśo jāyate
          tadā tatkṣaṇam eva pūrṇātmatālābhaḥ/ tad uktaṃ caturthe vimarśe — 
 
 tais tair apy upayācitair upanatas tasyāḥ sthito ’py antike 
 kānto lokasamāna evam aparijñāto na rantuṃ yathā/ 
 lokasyaiṣa tathānavekṣitaguṇaḥ svātmāpi viśveśvaro 
 naivālaṃ 
 naivālaṃ  ] Torella;  naivāyaṃ  A. 
  nijavaibhavāya tad iyaṃ tatpratyabhijñoditā// iti/ 
 
 [l. 8.148] 
 abhinavaguptādibhir ācāryair vihitapratāno ’py ayam arthaḥ saṃgraham upakramamāṇair
          asmābhir vistarabhiyā na pratānita iti sarvaṃ śivam// 
 iti sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe pratyabhijñādarśanam// 
 
 
        [atha raseśvaradarśanam //9//]

         [l. 9.1] 
 apare māheśvarāḥ parameśvaratādātmyavādino ’pi piṇḍasthairye sarvābhimatā jīvanmuktiḥ
          setsyatīty āsthāya piṇḍasthairyopāyaṃ pāradādipadavedanīyaṃ rasam eva saṃgirante/ 
 [l. 9.4] 
 rasasya pāradatvaṃ saṃsāraparapāraprāpaṇahetutvena/ tad uktam — 
 
 saṃsārasya paraṃ pāraṃ datte ’sau pāradaḥ smṛtaḥ/ iti/ 
 
 rasārṇave ’pi — 
 
 pārado gadito yasmāt parārthaṃ sādhakottamaiḥ/ 
 sūto 
 sūto  ]  Rasārṇava ;  supto  ASS, A, IV. 
  ’yaṃ matsamo devi mama pratyaṅgasaṃbhavaḥ// 
 mama deharaso yasmād rasas tenāyam ucyate/ iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.10] 
 
 nanu prakārāntareṇāpi jīvanmuktiyuktau neyaṃ vācoyuktir
            yuktimatīti cen na/ ṣaṭsv api darśaneṣu dehapātānantaraṃ mukter uktatayā tatra
            viśvāsānupapattyā nirvicikitsapravṛtter anupapatteḥ/ tad apy uktaṃ tatraiva — 
 
 
 ṣaḍdarśane ’pi muktis tu darśitā piṇḍapātane/ 
 karāmalakavat sāpi pratyakṣā nopalabhyate// 
 tasmāt taṃ rakṣayet piṇḍaṃ rasaiś caiva rasāyanaiḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.16] 
 govindabhagavatpādācāryair api — 
 
 iti dhanaśarīrabhogān matvānityān sadaiva yatanīyam/ 
 muktau sā ca jñānāt tac cābhyāsāt sa ca sthire dehe// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.19] 
 nanu vinaśvaratayā dṛśyamānasya dehasya kathaṃ nityatvam avasīyata iti cet — maivaṃ
          maṃsthāḥ/ ṣāṭkauśikasya śarīrasyānityatve ’pi rasābhrakapadābhilapyaharagaurīsṛṣṭijātasya
          nityatvopapatteḥ/ 
 [l. 9.22] 
 tathā ca rasahṛdaye — 
 
 ye cātyaktaśarīrā haragaurisṛṣṭijāṃ tanuṃ prāptāḥ/ 
 muktās te rasasiddhā mantragaṇaḥ kiṃkaro yeṣām// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.25] 
 tasmāj jīvanmuktiṃ samīhamānena yoginā prathamaṃ divyatanur vidheyā/
          haragaurīsṛṣṭisaṃyogajanitatvaṃ ca rasasya harajatvenābhrakasya gaurīsaṃbhavatvena
          tattadātmakatvam uktam — 
 
 abhrakas tava bījaṃ tu mama bījaṃ tu pāradaḥ/ 
 anayor melanaṃ devi mṛtyudāridryanāśanam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.30] 
 atyalpam idam ucyate devadaityamunimānavādiṣu bahavo rasasāmarthyād divyaṃ deham āśritya
          jīvanmuktim āśritāḥ śrūyante raseśvarasiddhānte — 
 
 devāḥ kecin maheśādyā daityāḥ kāvyapuraḥsarāḥ/ 
 munayo vālakhilyādyā nṛpāḥ someśvarādayaḥ// 
 govindabhagavatpādācāryo govindanāyakaḥ/ 
 carvaṭiḥ kapilo vyāliḥ kāpāliḥ kandalāyanaḥ// 
 etebhyo bahavaḥ siddhā jīvanmuktāś caranti hi/ 
 tanuṃ rasamayīṃ prāpya tadātmakakathācaṇāḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.38] 
 ayam evārthaḥ parameśvareṇa parameśvarīṃ prati prapañcitaḥ — 
 
 karmayogeṇa deveśi prāpyate piṇḍadhāraṇam/ 
 rasaś ca pavanaś ceti karmayogo dvidhā smṛtaḥ// 
 mūrchito harati vyādhīn mṛto jīvayati svayam/ 
 baddhaḥ khecaratāṃ kuryād raso vāyuś ca bhairavi// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.43] 
 mūrchitasvarūpam uktam — 
 
 nānāvarṇo bhavet sūto vihāya ghanacāpalam/ 
 lakṣaṇaṃ dṛśyate yasya mūrchitaṃ taṃ vadanti hi// 
 ārdratvaṃ ca ghanatvaṃ ca tejogauravacāpalam/ 
 yasyaitāni na dṛśyante taṃ vidyān mṛtasūtakam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.48] 
 anyatra baddhasvarūpam apy abhyadhāyi — 
 
 akṣataś ca laghudrāvī tejasvī nirmalo guruḥ/ 
 sphoṭanaṃ punar āvṛttau baddhasūtasya lakṣaṇam/ iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.51] 
 nanu haragaurīsṛṣṭisiddhau piṇḍasthairyam āsthātuṃ pāryate/ tatsiddhir eva katham iti cet
          — na aṣṭādaśasaṃskāravaśāt tadupapatteḥ/ tad uktam ācāryaiḥ — 
 
 tasya prasādhanavidhau sudhiyā pratikarmanirmalāḥ prathamam/ 
 aṣṭādaśa saṃskārā vijñātavyāḥ prayatnena// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.55] 
 te ca saṃskārā nirūpitāḥ — 
 
 svedanamardanamūrchanasthāpanapātananirodhaniyamāś ca/ 
 dīpanagaganagrāsapramāṇam atha jāraṇapidhānam// 
 garbhadrutibāhyadrutikṣāraṇasaṃrāgasāraṇāś caiva/ 
 krāmaṇavedhau bhakṣaṇam aṣṭādaśadheti rasakarma// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.60] 
 tatprapañcas tu govindabhagavatpādācāryasarvajñarāmeśvarabhaṭṭārakaprabhṛtibhiḥ prācīnair
          ācāryair nirūpita iti granthabhūyastvabhayād udāsyate/ na ca rasaśāstraṃ dhātuvādārtham
          eveti mantavyam/ dehavedhadvārā mukter eva paramaprayojanatvāt/ tad uktaṃ rasārṇave — 
 
 lohavedhas tvayā deva yadartham upavarṇitaḥ/ 
 taṃ dehavedham ācakṣva yena syāt khecarī gatiḥ// 
 yathā lohe tathā dehe kartavyaḥ sūtakaḥ satā/ 
 samānaṃ kurute devi pratyayaṃ dehalohayoḥ/ 
 pūrvaṃ lohe parīkṣeta paścād dehe prayojayet// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.69] 
 nanu saccidānandātmakaparatattvasphuraṇād eva muktisiddhau kim anena
          divyadehasaṃpādanaprayāseneti cet — tad etad vārttam/ avārttaśarīrālābhe 
 avārtta ° ];  vārtta  IV;  avārta  A, ASS. 
  tadvārttāyā 
 ° vārttāyā  ] IV; ° vārtāyā  A, ASS. 
  ayogāt/ tad uktaṃ rasahṛdaye — 
 
 galitānalpavikalpaḥ sarvādhvavivakṣitaś cidānandaḥ/ 
 sphurito ’py asphuritatanoḥ karoti kiṃ jantuvargasya// iti/ 
 yaj jarayā jarjaritaṃ kāsaśvāsādiduḥkhaviśadaṃ ca/ 
 yogyaṃ yan na samādhau pratihatabuddhīndriyaprasaram// iti/ 
 bālaḥ ṣoḍaśavarṣo viṣayarasāsvādalampaṭaḥ parataḥ/ 
 yātaviveko vṛddho martyaḥ katham āpnuyān muktim// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.80] 
 nanu jīvatvaṃ nāma saṃsāritvam/ tadviparītatvaṃ muktatvam/ tathā ca parasparaviruddhayoḥ
          katham ekāyatanatvam upapannaṃ syād iti cet — tad anupapannam/ vikalpānupapatteḥ/ muktis
          tāvat sarvatīrthakarasaṃmatā/ sā kiṃ jñeyapade niviśate na vā/ carame śaśaviṣāṇakalpā
          syāt/ prathame na jīvanaṃ varjanīyam/ ajīvato jñātṛtvānupapatteḥ/ tad uktaṃ
          raseśvarasiddhānte/ 
 
 rasāṅkameyamārgokto jīvamokṣo ’nyathā tu na/ 
 pramāṇāntaravādeṣu yuktibhedāvalambiṣu// 
 jñātṛjñeyam idaṃ viddhi sarvatantreṣu saṃmatam/ 
 nājīvañ jñāsyati jñeyaṃ yad ato ’sty eva jīvanam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.90] 
 na cedam adṛṣṭacaram iti mantavyam/ viṣṇusvāmimatānusāribhir nṛpañcāsyaśarīrasya
          nityatvopapādanāt/ tad uktaṃ sākārasiddhau — 
 
 saccinnityanijācintyapūrṇānandaikavigraham/ 
 nṛpañcāsyam ahaṃ vande śrīviṣṇusvāmisaṃmatam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.94] 
 nanv etat sāvayavaṃ rūpavad avabhāsamānaṃ nṛkaṇṭhīravāṅgaṃ sad iti na saṃgacchata
          ityādinākṣepapuraḥsaraṃ sanakādipratyakṣa 
 sanakādipratyakṣa  ];  sanakādipratyakṣaṃ  A, ASS, IV. 
  — sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ ityādiśruti — 
 
 tam adbhutaṃ bālakam ambujekṣaṇaṃ caturbhujaṃ śaṅkhagadādyudāyudham/ 
 
 ityādipurāṇalakṣaṇena pramāṇatrayeṇa siddhaṃ nṛpañcānanāṅgaṃ katham asat syād iti/
          sadādīni viśeṣaṇāni garbhaśrīkāntamiśrair viṣṇusvāmicaraṇapariṇatāntaḥkaraṇaiḥ
          pratipāditāni/ tasmād asmadiṣṭadehanityatvam atyantādṛṣṭaṃ na bhavatīti puruṣārthakāmukaiḥ
          puruṣair eṣṭavyam/ ata evoktam — 
 
 āyatanaṃ vidyānāṃ mūlaṃ dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇām/ 
 śreyaḥ paraṃ kim anyac charīram ajarāmaraṃ vihāyaikam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.106] 
 ajarāmarīkaraṇasamarthaś ca rasendra eva/ tad āha — 
 
 eko ’sau rasarājaḥ śarīram ajarāmaraṃ kurute/ iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.108] 
 kiṃ varṇyate rasasya māhātmyam/ darśanasparśanādināpi mahat phalaṃ bhavati/ tad uktaṃ
          rasārṇave — 
 
 darśanāt sparśanāt tasya bhakṣaṇāt smaraṇād api// 
 pūjanād rasadānāc ca dṛśyate ṣaḍvidhaṃ phalam// 
 kedārādīni liṅgāni pṛthivyāṃ yāni kānicit// 
 tāni dṛṣṭvā tu yat puṇyaṃ tat puṇyaṃ rasadarśanāt/ ityādinā/ 
 
 [l. 9.114] 
 anyatrāpi — 
 
 kāśyādisarvaliṅgebhyo rasaliṅgārcanāc chivaḥ/ 
 prāpyate yena tal liṅgaṃ bhogārogyāmṛtapradam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9. 117] 
 rasanindāyāḥ pratyavāyo ’pi darśitaḥ — 
 
 pramādād rasanindāyāḥ śrutāv enaṃ smaret sudhīḥ/ 
 drāk tyajen nindakaṃ nityaṃ nindayā pūritāśubham// iti/ 
 
 [l. 9.120] 
 tasmād asmaduktayā rītyā divyaṃ dehaṃ saṃpādya yogābhyāsavaśāt paratattve dṛṣṭe
          puruṣārthaprāptir bhavati/ tadā — 
 
 bhrūyugamadhyagataṃ yac chikhividyutsūryavaj jagadbhāsi/ 
 keṣāṃcit puṇyadṛśām unmīlati cinmayaṃ jyotiḥ// 
 paramānandaikarasaṃ paramaṃ jyotiḥsvabhāvam avikalpam/ 
 vigalitasakalakleśaṃ jñeyaṃ śāntaṃ svasaṃvedyam/ 
 tasminn ādhāya manaḥ sphurad akhilaṃ cinmayaṃ jagat paśyan/ 
 utsannakarmabandho brahmatvam ihaiva cāpnoti// 
 
 [l. 9.129] 
 śrutiś ca — raso vai saḥ/ rasaṃ hy evāyaṃ labdhvānandī bhavati iti/ tad itthaṃ
          bhavadainyaduḥkhabharataraṇopāyo rasa eveti siddham/ tathā ca rasasya parabrahmaṇā sāmyam
          iti pratipādakaḥ ślokaḥ — 
 
 yaḥ syāt prāvaraṇāvimocanadhiyāṃ sādhyaḥ prakṛtyā punaḥ 
 saṃpannaḥ sahate na dīvyati paraṃ vaiśvānare jāgrati/ 
 jñāto yady aparaṃ na vedayati ca svasmāt svayaṃ dyotate 
 yo brahmaiva 
 brahmaiva  ] ASS, IV;  brahmeva  A. 
  sa dainyasaṃsṛtibhayāt pāyād asau pāradaḥ// iti// 
 
 iti sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe raseśvaradarśanam 
 raseśvaradarśanam  ];  raseśvaradaṛśanam  A. 
 
 
 
        [athaulūkyadarśanam //10//]

         [l. 10.1] 
 iha khalu nikhilaprekṣāvān nisargapratikūlavedanīyatayā nikhilātmasaṃvedanasiddhaṃ
          duḥkhaṃ jihāsus taddhānopāyaṃ jijnāsuḥ parameśvarasākṣātkāram upāyam ākalayati/ 
 
 yadā carmavad ākāśaṃ veṣṭayiṣyanti mānavāḥ/ 
 tadā śivam avijñāya duḥkhasyānto bhaviṣyati// 
 
 ityādivacananicayaprāmāṇyāt/ parameśvarasākṣātkāraś ca śravaṇamananabhāvanābhir
          bhāvanīyaḥ/ yad āha — 
 
 āgamenānumānena dhyānābhyāsabalena ca/ 
 tridhā prakalpayan prajñāṃ labhate yogam uttamam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 10.10] 
 tatra mananam anumānādhīnam/ anumānaṃ ca vyāptijñānādhīnam/ vyāptijñānaṃ ca
          padārthavivekasāpekṣam/ ataḥ padārthaṣaṭkam athāto dharmaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ityādikāyāṃ
          daśalakṣaṇyāṃ kaṇabhakṣeṇa bhagavatā vyavasthāpitam/ 
 [l. 10.14] 
 tatrāhnikadvayātmake prathame ’dhyāye samavetāśeṣapadārthakathanam akāri/ tatrāpi
          prathamāhnike jātimannirūpaṇam/ dvitīyāhnike jātiviśeṣayor nirūpaṇam/ āhnikadvayayukte
          dvitīye ’dhyāye dravyanirūpaṇam/ tatrāpi prathamāhnike bhūtaviśeṣalakṣaṇam/ dvitīye
          dikkālapratipādanam/ āhnikadvayayukte tṛtīya ātmāntaḥkaraṇalakṣaṇam/ tatrāpy ātmalakṣaṇaṃ
          prathame/ dvitīye ’ntaḥkaraṇalakṣaṇam/ āhnikadvayayukte caturthe
          śarīratadupayogivivecanam/ atrāpi prathame tadupayogivivecanam/ dvitīye śarīravivecanam/
          āhnikadvayavati pañcame karmapratipādanam/ tatrāpi prathame śarīrasaṃbandhikarmacintanam/
          dvitīye mānasakarmacintanam/ āhnikadvayaśālini ṣaṣṭhe śrautadharmanirūpaṇam/ tatrāpi
          prathame dānapratigrahadharmavivekaḥ/ dvitīye cāturāśramyocitadharmanirūpaṇam/ tathāvidhe
          saptame guṇasamavāyapratipādanam/ tatrāpi prathame buddhinirapekṣaguṇapratipādanam/
          dvitīye tatsāpekṣaguṇapratipādanaṃ samavāyapratipādanaṃ ca/ aṣṭame
          nirvikalpakasavikalpakapratyakṣapramāṇacintanam/ navame buddhiviśeṣapratipādanam/ daśame
          ’numānabhedapratipādanam/ 
 [l. 10.30] 
 tatroddeśo lakṣaṇaṃ parīkṣā ceti trividhāsya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ/ nanu vibhāgāpekṣayā
          cāturvidhye vaktavye kathaṃ traividhyam uktam iti cet — maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ/ vibhāgasya
          viśeṣoddeśarūpatvād uddeśa evāntarbhāvāt/ tatra dravyaguṇakarmasāmānyaviśeṣasamavāyā iti
          ṣaḍ eva te padārthā ity uddeśaḥ/ kim atra kramaniyame kāraṇam/ ucyate/
          samastapadārthāyatanatvena pradhānasya dravyasya prathamam uddeśaḥ/ anantaraṃ
          guṇatvopādhinā sakaladravyavṛtter guṇasya/ tadanu sāmānyavattvasāmyāt karmaṇaḥ/ paścāt
          tattritayāśritasya sāmānyasya/ tadanantaraṃ samavāyādhikaraṇasya viśeṣasya/ ante
          ’vaśiṣṭasya samavāyasyeti/ 
 [l. 10.39] 
 nanu ṣaḍ eva padārthā iti kathaṃ kathyate/ abhāvasyāpi sadbhāvād iti cet — maivaṃ vocaḥ/
          nañarthānullikhitadhīviṣayatayā bhāvarūpatayā ṣaḍ eveti vivakṣitatvāt/ tathāpi kathaṃ ṣaḍ
          eveti niyama upapadyate/ vikalpānupapatteḥ/ tathā hi/ niyamavyavacchedyaṃ pramitaṃ na vā/
          pramitatve kathaṃ niṣedhaḥ/ apramitatve kathaṃtarām/ na hi kaścit prekṣāvān mūṣikaviṣāṇaṃ
          pratiṣeddhuṃ yatate/ tataś cānupapatter na niyama iti cet — maivaṃ bhāṣiṣṭhāḥ/ saptamatayā
          pramite ’ndhakārādau bhāvatvasya bhāvatayā pramite śaktisādṛśyādau saptamatvasya ca
          niṣedhād iti kṛtaṃ vistareṇa/ 
 [l. 10.47] 
 tatra dravyāditritayasya dravyatvādijātir lakṣaṇam/ dravyatvaṃ nāma
          gaganāravindasamavetatve sati nityatve sati gandhāsamavetatvam/ guṇatvaṃ nāma
          samavāyikāraṇāsamavetāsamavāyikāraṇabhinnasamavetasatttāsākṣād- vyāpyajātiḥ/ karmatvaṃ
          nāma nityāsamavetatvasahitasattāsākṣādvyāpyajātiḥ/ sāmānyaṃ tu
          pradhvaṃsapratiyogitvarahitam anekasamavetam/ viśeṣo nāmānyonyābhāvavirodhisāmānyarahitaḥ
          samavetaḥ/ samavāyas tu samavāyarahitaḥ saṃbandha iti ṣaṇṇāṃ lakṣaṇāni vyavasthitāni/ 
 [l. 10.54] 
 dravyaṃ navavidhaṃ pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśakāladigātmamanāṃsīti/ tatra
          pṛthivyādicatuṣṭayasya pṛthivītvādijātir lakṣaṇam/ pṛthivītvaṃ nāma
          pākajarūpasamānādhikaraṇadravyatvasākṣādvyāpyajātiḥ/ aptvaṃ nāma saritsāgarasamavetatve
          sati jvalanāsamavetaṃ sāmānyam/ tejastvaṃ nāma candracāmīkarasamavetatve sati
          salilāsamavetaṃ sāmānyam/ vāyutvaṃ nāma tvagindriyasamavetadravyatvasākṣādvyāpyajātiḥ/
          ākāśakāladiśām ekaikatvād aparajātyabhāve pāribhāṣikyas tisraḥ saṃjñā bhavanti ākāśaḥ kālo
          dig iti/ saṃyogājanyajanyaviśeṣaguṇasamānādhikaraṇaviśeṣādhikaraṇam ākāśam/ vibhutve sati
          digasamavetaparatvāsamavāyikāraṇādhikaraṇaḥ kālaḥ/ akālatve saty aviśeṣaguṇā mahatī dik/
          ātmamanasor ātmatvamanastve/ ātmatvaṃ nāmāmūrtasamavetadravyatvāparajātiḥ/ manastvaṃ nāma
          dravyasamavāyikāraṇatvarahitāṇusamavetadravyatvāparajātiḥ/ 
 [l. 10.67] 
 rūparasagandhasparśasaṃkhyāparimāṇapṛthaktvasaṃyogavibhāga-paratvāparatvabuddhisukhaduḥkhecchādveṣaprayatnāś

 [l. 10.81] 
 
 dvitve ca pākajotpattau vibhāge ca vibhāgaje/ 
 yasya na skhalitā buddhis taṃ vai vaiśeṣikaṃ viduḥ// 
 
 ity ābhāṇakasya sadbhāvād dvitvādyutpattiprakāraḥ pradarśyate/ tatra prathamam
          indriyārthasaṃnikarṣaḥ (1)/ tasmād ekatvasāmānyajñānam (2)/ tato ’pekṣābuddhiḥ (3)/ tato

          dravye iti dhīḥ (7)/ tataḥ saṃskāraḥ/ tad āha — 
 
 ādāv indriyasaṃnikarṣaghaṭanād ekatvasāmānyadhīr 
 ekatvobhayagocarā matir ato dvitvaṃ tato jāyate/ 
 dvitvatvapramitis tato nu parato dvitvapramānantaraṃ 
 dve dravye iti dhīr iyaṃ nigaditā dvitvodayaprakriyā// iti/ 
 
 dvitvāder apekṣābuddhijanyatve kiṃ pramāṇam/ atrāhur ācāryāḥ — apekṣābuddhir dvitvāder
          utpādikā bhavitum arhati/ vyañjakatvānupapattau tenānuvidhīyamānatvāt/ śabdaṃ prati
          saṃyogavad iti/ vayaṃ tu brūmaḥ — dvitvādikam ekatvadvayaviṣayānityabuddhivyaṅgyaṃ na
          bhavati anekāśritaguṇatvāt pṛthaktvādivad iti/ 
 [l. 10.97] 
 nivṛttikramo nirūpyate — apekṣābuddhita ekatvasāmānyajñānasya dvitvotpattisamakālaṃ
          nivṛttiḥ/ apekṣābuddher dvitvatvasāmānyajñānād dvitvaguṇabuddhisamasamayam/
          dvitvasyāpekṣābuddhinivṛtter dravyabuddhisamakālam/ guṇabuddher dravyabuddhitaḥ
          saṃskārotpattisamakālam/ dravyabuddhes tadanantaraṃ saṃskārād iti/ 
 tathā ca saṃgrahaślokāḥ — 
 
 ādāv apekṣābuddhyā hi naśyed ekatvajātidhīḥ/ 
 dvitvodayasamaṃ paścāt sā ca tajjātibuddhitaḥ// 
 dvitvākhyaguṇadhīkāle tato dvitvaṃ nivartate/ 
 apekṣābuddhināśena dravyadhījanmakālataḥ//

 dravyabuddhiś ca saṃskārād iti nāśakramo mataḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 10.108] 
 buddher buddhyantaravināśyatve saṃskāravināśyatve ca pramāṇam — vivādādhyāsitāni jñānāny

 [l. 10.114] 
 atha dvyaṇukanāśam ārabhya katibhiḥ kṣaṇaiḥ punar anyad dvyaṇukam utpadya rūpādimad

          dravyārambhaṇāya kriyā/ tayā pūrvadeśād vibhāgaḥ/ vibhāgena pūrvadeśasaṃyoganivṛttiḥ/

          pīlupākaprakriyā/ piṭharapākaprakriyā naiyāyikadhīsaṃmatā/ 
 [l. 10.125] 
 vibhāgajavibhāgo dvividhaḥ — kāraṇamātravibhāgajaḥ kāraṇākāraṇavibhāgajaś ca/ tatra

 dvitīyas tu haste karmotpannam avayavāntarād vibhāgaṃ akurvad

 [l. 10.153] 
 gandhādivyāptasya nīlarūpasya tannivṛttau nivṛtteḥ/ 
 atha nīlaṃ tama iti gateḥ kā gatir iti cet 
 nīlaṃ nabha itivad bhrāntir evety alaṃ vṛddhavīvadhayā/ ata eva nāropitarūpaṃ tamaḥ/

          vyabhicārāt/ na cābhāve bhāvadharmādhyāropo durupapādaḥ/ duḥkhābhāve sukhatvāropasya
          saṃyogābhāve vibhāgatvābhimānasya ca dṛṣṭatvāt/

          rūpavadabhāvatvenālokasāpekṣacakṣurjanyajñānaviṣayatvaṃ syād ity eṣitavyam/ yadgrahe

          abhāvena tadabhāvagrahe 'pi tadapekṣāyā abhāvāt/

          dravyaguṇakarmaniṣpattivaidharmyād abhāvas tamaḥ iti

         [l. 11.1] 
 tattvajñānād duḥkhātyantocchedalakṣaṇaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ bhavatīti samānatantre 'pi
          pratipāditam/ tad āha sūtrakāraḥ — pramāṇaprameyetyāditattvajñānān niḥśreyasādhigama iti/
          idaṃ nyāyaśāstrasyādimaṃ sūtram/ nyāyaśāstraṃ ca pañcādhyāyātmakam/ tatra pratyadhyāyam
          āhnikadvayam/ tatra prathamādhyāyasya prathamāhnike bhagavatā gautamena
          pramāṇādipadārthanavakalakṣaṇanirūpaṇaṃ vidhāya dvitīye
          vādādisaptapadārthalakṣaṇanirūpaṇaṃ kṛtam/ dvitīyasya prathame saṃśayaparīkṣaṇaṃ
          pramāṇacatuṣṭayāprāmāṇyaśaṅkānirākaraṇam/ dvitīye 'rthāpattyāder antarbhāvanirūpaṇam/
          tṛtīyasya prathama ātmaśarīrendriyārthaparīkṣaṇam/ dvitīye buddhimanaḥparīkṣaṇam/
          caturthasya prathame pravṛttidoṣapretyabhāvaphaladuḥkhāpavargaparīkṣaṇam/ dvitīye
          doṣanimittakatvanirūpaṇam avayavyādinirūpaṇaṃ ca/ pañcamasya prathame jātibhedanirūpaṇam/
          dvitīye nigrahasthānabhedanirūpaṇam/ 
 [l. 11.14] 
 mānādhīnā meyasiddhir iti nyāyena pramāṇasya prathamam uddeśe tadanusāreṇa lakṣaṇasya
          kathanīyatayā prathamoddiṣṭasya pramāṇasya prathamaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kathyate —
          sādhanāśrayāvyatiriktatve sati pramāvyāptaṃ pramāṇam/ evaṃ ca pratitantrasiddhāntasiddhaṃ
          parameśvaraprāmāṇyaṃ saṃgṛhītaṃ bhavati/ yad acakathat sūtrakāraḥ —
          mantrāyurvedaprāmāṇyavac ca tatprāmāṇyam āptaprāmāṇyāt iti/ tathā ca
          nyāyanayapārāvārapāradṛśvā viśvavikhyātakīrtir udayanācāryo 'pi nyāyakusumāñjalau caturthe
          stabake — 
 
 mitiḥ samyakparicchittis tadvattā ca pramātṛtā/

 [l. 11.76] 
 nanu tattvajñānān niḥśresayaṃ bhavatīty uktam/ tatra kiṃ tattvajñānād anantaram eva
          niḥśresayaṃ saṃpadyate/ nety ucyate/ kiṃ tu tattvajñānād

          mithyājñānaṃ nāmānātmani dehādāv ātmabuddhiḥ/ tadanukūleṣu rāgaḥ/ tatpratikūleṣu dveṣaḥ/
          vastutas tv ātmanaḥ pratikūlam anukūlaṃ vā na kiṃcid vastv asti/ parasparānubandhitvāc ca

          preritaḥ prāṇī pratiṣiddhāni śarīreṇa hiṃsāsteyādīny ācarati/ vācā anṛtādīni/ manasā
          paradrohādīni/ seyaṃ pāparūpā pravṛttir adharmaḥ/ śarīreṇa praśastāni
          dānaparaparitrāṇādīni/ vācā hitasatyādīni/ manasā ajighāṃsādīni/ seyaṃ puṇyarūpā pravṛttir
          dharmaḥ/ seyam ubhayī pravṛttiḥ/ tataḥ svānurūpaṃ praśastaṃ ninditaṃ vā janma punaḥ
          śarīrādeḥ prādurbhāvaḥ/ tasmin sati pratikūlavedanīyatayā bādhanātmakaṃ duḥkhaṃ bhavati/
          [na hy apravṛttasya duḥkhaṃ pratyāpadyata iti kaścit prapadyate/] 
 This sentence is missing in IV p. 115. 
  ta ime mithyājñānādayo duḥkhāntā avicchedena pravartamānāḥ saṃsāraśabdārtho
          ghaṭīcakravan niravadhir anuvartate/ yadā kaścit puruṣadhaureyaḥ
          purākṛtasukṛtaparipākavaśād ācāryopadeśena sarvam idaṃ duḥkhāyatanaṃ duḥkhānuṣaktaṃ ca
          paśyati tadā tat sarvaṃ heyatvena budhyate/ tatas tannirvartakam avidyādi nivartayitum
          icchati/ tannivṛttyupāyaś ca tattvajñānam iti/ kasyacic catasṛbhir vibhaktaṃ prameyaṃ
          bhāvayataḥ samyagdarśanapadavedanīyatayā tattvajñānaṃ jāyate/ tattvajñānān mithyājñānam
          apaiti/ mithyājñānāpāye doṣā apayānti/ doṣāpāye pravṛttir apaiti/ pravṛttyapāye
          janmāpaiti/ janmāpāye duḥkham atyantaṃ nivartate/ sātyantikī duḥkhanivṛttir apavargaḥ/
          nivṛtter ātyantikatvaṃ nāma nivartyasajātīyasya punas tatrānutpāda iti/ tathā ca
          pāramarṣaṃ sūtram — duḥkhajanmapravṛttidoṣamithyājñānānām uttarottarāpāye tadanantarāpāyād
          apavargaḥ iti/ 
 [l. 11.103] 
 nanu duḥkhātyantocchedo 'pavarga ity etad adyāpi kaphoṇiguḍāyitaṃ vartate/ tat kathaṃ
          siddhavatkṛtya vyavahriyate iti cet — 
 maivam/ sarveṣāṃ mokṣavādinām apavargadaśāyām ātyantikī duḥkhanivṛttir astīty asyārthasya
          sarvatantrasiddhāntasiddhatayā ghaṇṭāpathatvāt/ 
 tathā hi — ātmocchedo mokṣa iti mādhyamikamate duḥkhocchedo 'stīty etāvat tāvad avivādam/
          atha manyethāḥ — śarīrādivad ātmāpi duḥkhahetutvād ucchedya iti tan na saṃgacchate/

          nivṛttir aśakyavidhānaiva/ anityatve pravṛttyanupapattiḥ/ vyavahārānupapattiś cādhikaṃ
          dūṣaṇam/ na khalu kaścit prekṣāvān ātmanas tu kāmāya sarvaṃ priyaṃ bhavatīti sarvataḥ
          priyatamasyātmanaḥ samucchedāya prayatate/ sarvo hi prāṇī sati dharmiṇi mukta iti
          vyavaharati nanu/ 
 dharminivṛttau nirmalajñānodayo mahodaya iti vijñānavādivāde sāmagryabhāvaḥ
          sāmānādhikaraṇyānupapattiś ca/ bhāvanācatuṣṭayaṃ hi tasya kāraṇam abhīṣṭam/ tac ca
          kṣaṇabhaṅgapakṣe sthiraikādhārāsaṃbhavāl laṅghanābhyāsādivad anāsāditaprakarṣaṃ na sphuṭam

 āvaraṇamuktir muktir iti jainajanābhimato 'pi mārgo na nisargato nirargalaḥ/ aṅga bhavān
          pṛṣṭo vyācaṣṭām kim āvaraṇam/ dharmādharmabhrāntaya iti cet — iṣṭam eva/ atha deham
          evāvaraṇam/ tathā ca tannivṛttau pañjarān muktasya śukasyevātmanaḥ satatordhvagamanaṃ
          muktir iti cet — tadā vaktavyam/ kim ayam ātmā mūrto 'mūrto vā/ prathame niravayavaḥ
          sāvayavo vā/ niravayavatve niravayavo mūrtaḥ paramāṇur iti paramāṇulakṣaṇāpattyā
          paramāṇudharmavad ātmadharmāṇām atīndriyatvaṃ prasajyeta/ sāvayavatve yat sāvayavaṃ tad
          anityam iti pratibandhabalenānityatvāpattau kṛtapraṇāśākṛtābhyāgamau niṣpratibandhau
          prasaretām/ amūrtatve gamanam anupapannam eva/ calanātmikāyāḥ kriyāyā
          mūrtatvapratibandhāt/ 
 pāratantryaṃ bandhaḥ svātantryaṃ mokṣa iti cārvākapakṣe 'pi svātantryaṃ duḥkhanivṛttiś
          cet — avivādaḥ/ aiśvaryaṃ cet — sātiśayatayā sadṛkṣatayā ca prekṣāvatāṃ nābhimatam/ 
 prakṛtipuruṣānyatvakhyātau prakṛtyuparame puruṣasya svarūpeṇāvasthānaṃ muktir iti
          sāṃkhyākhyāte 'pi pakṣe duḥkhocchedo 'sty eva/ vivekajñānaṃ puruṣāśrayaṃ prakṛtyāśrayaṃ
          vety etāvad avaśiṣyate/ tatra puruṣāśrayam iti na śliṣyate/ puruṣasya
          kauṭasthyāvasthānanirodhāpātāt/ nāpi prakṛtir āśrayaḥ 
 prakṛtir āśrayaḥ  ];  prakṛtyāśrayaḥ  ASS, IV, A. The masculine compound  prakṛtyāśrayaḥ  (in all editions) makes no sense. The
              preceding context favors neuter  prakṛtyāśrayam .
              However, since there is a back reference to feminine  prakṛti  in the immediately following sentence, I have accepted the reading  prakṛtirāśrayaḥ. 
 / acetanatvāt tasyāḥ/ kiṃ ca prakṛtiḥ pravṛttisvabhāvā nivṛttisvabhāvā vā/ ādye

          tathābhāvaprasaṅgāt/
