 [l. 15.159] 
 ata eva kecana yujiṃ samādhāv api paṭhanti yuja samādhāv iti/ nāpi
          yājñavalkyavacanavyākopaḥ/ tatrasthasyāpi yogaśabdasya samādhyarthatvāt/ 
 
 samādhiḥ samatāvasthā jīvātmaparamātmanoḥ/ 
 brahmaṇy eva sthitir yā sā samādhiḥ pratyagātmanaḥ// 
 
 iti tenaivoktatvāc ca/ tad uktaṃ bhagavatā vyāsena yogaḥ samādhir iti/ 
 [l. 15.166] 
 nanv evam aṣṭāṅgayoge caramasyāṅgasya samādhitvam uktaṃ patañjalinā
          yamaniyamāsanaprāṇāyāmapratyāhāradhāraṇādhyānasamādhayo 'ṣṭāv aṅgāni yogasyeti/ na cāṅgy
          evāṅgatām gantum utsahate/ upakāryopakārakabhāvasya darśapūrṇamāsaprayājādau
          bhinnāyatanatvenātyantabhedāt/ ataḥ samādhir api na yogaśabdārtho yujyata iti cet — tan na
          yujyate/ vyutpattimātrābhidhitsayā tad evārthamātranirbhāsaṃ svarūpaśūnyam iva samādhiḥ
          iti nirūpitacaramāṅgavācakena samādhiśabdenāṅgino yogasyābhedavivakṣayā vyapadeśopapatteḥ/
          na ca vyutpattibalād eva sarvatra śabdaḥ pravartate/ tathātve gacchatīti gaur iti
          vyutpattes tiṣṭhan gaur na syāt/ gacchan devadattaś ca gauḥ syāt/ 
 [l. 15.176] 
 pravṛttinimittaṃ ca prāg uktam eva cittavṛttinirodha iti/ tad uktaṃ yogaś
          cittavṛttinirodhaḥ iti/ 
 [l. 15.178] 
 nanu vṛttīnaṃ nirodhaś ced yogo 'bhimatas tāsāṃ jñānatvenātmāśrayatayā tannirodho 'pi
          pradhvaṃsapadavedanīyas tadāśrayo bhavet/ prāgabhāvapradhvaṃsayoḥ
          pratiyogisamānāśrayatvaniyamāt/ tataś ca 
 
 upayann apayan dharmo vikaroti hi dharmiṇam/ 
 
 iti nyāyenātmanaḥ kauṭasthyaṃ vihanyeteti cet — tad api na ghaṭate/
          nirodhapratiyogibhūtānāṃ pramāṇaviparyayavikalpanidrāsmṛtisvarūpāṇāṃ vṛttīnām
          antaḥkaraṇādyaparaparyāyacittadharmatvāṅgīkārāt/ kūṭasthanityā cicchaktir apariṇāminī
          vijñānadharmāśrayo bhavituṃ nārhaty eva/ na ca citiśakter apariṇāmitvam asiddham iti
          mantavyam/ citiśaktir apariṇāminī sadā jñātṛtvāt/ na yad evaṃ na tad evaṃ yathā cittādi —
          ityādyanumānasaṃbhavāt/ tathā yady asau puruṣaḥ pariṇāmī syāt tadā pariṇāmasya
          kādācitkatvāt tāsāṃ cittavṛttīnāṃ sadā jñātatvaṃ nopapadyeta/ cidrūpasya puruṣasya
          sadaivādhiṣṭhātṛtvenāvasthitasya yad antaraṅgaṃ nirmalaṃ sattvaṃ tasyāpi sadaiva
          sthitatvāt yena yenārthenoparaktaṃ bhavati tasya dṛśyasya sadaiva cicchāyāpattyā
          bhānopapattyā puruṣasya niḥsaṅgatvaṃ saṃbhavati/ tataś ca siddhaṃ tasya sadā jñātṛtvam iti
          na kadācit pariṇāmitvaśaṅkāvatarati/ cittaṃ punar yena viṣayeṇoparaktaṃ bhavati sa viṣayo
          jñātaḥ yenoparaktaṃ na bhavati tad ajñātam iti vastuno 'yaskāntamaṇikalpasya
          jñānājñānakāraṇabhūtoparāgānuparāgadharmitvād ayaḥsadharmakaṃ cittaṃ pariṇāmīty
          ucyate/ 
 [l. 15.198] 
 nanu cittasyendriyāṇāṃ cāhaṃkārikāṇāṃ sarvagatatvāt sarvaviṣayair asti sadā saṃbandhaḥ/
          tathā ca sarveṣāṃ sarvadā sarvatra jñānaṃ prasajyeteti cet — na/ sarvagatatve 'pi cittaṃ
          yatra śarīre vṛttimat tena śarīreṇa saha saṃbandho yeṣāṃ viṣayāṇāṃ teṣv evāsya jñānaṃ
          bhavati netareṣv atyatiprasaṅgābhāvāt/ ata evāyaskāntamaṇikalpā viṣayā ayaḥsadharmakaṃ
          cittam indriyapraṇālikayābhisaṃbadhyo 
 ° bhisaṃbadhyo ° ] IV; ° bhisaṃbandhyo ° A. 
 parañjayantīty uktam/ tasmāc cittasya dharmā vṛttayo nātmanaḥ/ tathā ca śrutiḥ —
          kāmaḥ saṃkalpo vicikitsā śraddhāśraddhā dhṛtir adhṛtir hrīr dhīr bhīr ity etat sarvaṃ mana
          eva iti/ cicchakter apariṇāmitvaṃ pañcaśikhācāryair ākhyāyi — apariṇāminī bhoktṛśaktir
          iti/ patañjalināpi sadā jñātāś cittavṛttayas tatprabhoḥ puruṣasyāpariṇāmitvāt iti/
          cittapariṇāmitve 'numānam ucyate — cittaṃ pariṇāmi jñātājñātaviṣayatvāt śrotrādivad
          iti/ 
 [l. 15.210] 
 pariṇāmaś ca trividhaḥ prasiddho dharmalakṣaṇāvasthābhedāt/ 
 ° bhedāt/  ] ASS; ° bhedāt  IV, A. 
  dharmiṇaś cittasya nīlādyālocanaṃ dharmapariṇāmaḥ/ yathā kanakasya
          kaṭakamukuṭakeyūrādi/ dharmasya vartamānatvādir lakṣaṇapariṇāmaḥ/ nīlādyālocanasya
          sphuṭatvādir avasthāpariṇāmaḥ/ kaṭakādes tu navapurāṇatvādir avasthāpariṇāmaḥ/ evam
          anyatrāpi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pariṇāmatritayam ūhanīyam/ tathā ca pramāṇādivṛttīnaṃ
          cittadharmatvāt tannirodho 'pi tadāśraya eveti na kiṃcid anupapannam/ 
 [l. 15.217] 
 nanu vṛttinirodho yoga ity aṅgīkāre suṣuptyādau kṣiptamūḍhādicittavṛttīnāṃ
          nirodhasaṃbhavād yogatvaprasaṅgaḥ/ na caitad yujyate/ kṣiptādyavasthāsu kleśaprahāṇāder
          asaṃbhavān niḥśreyasaparipanthitvāc ca/ tathā hi — kṣiptaṃ nāma teṣu teṣu viṣayeṣu
          kṣipyamāṇam asthiraṃ cittam ucyate/ tamaḥsamudre magnaṃ nidrāvṛttibhāvitaṃ mūḍham iti
          gīyate/ kṣiptād viśiṣṭaṃ cittaṃ vikṣiptam iti gīyate/ viśeṣo nāma 
 
 cañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa pramāthi balavad dṛḍham/ 
 
 iti nyāyenāsthirasyāpi manasaḥ kādācitkasamudbhūtaviṣayasthairyasaṃbhavena sthairyam/
          asthiratvaṃ ca svābhāvikaṃ vyādhyādyanuśayajanitaṃ vā/ tad āha —
          vyādhistyānasaṃśayapramādālasyāviratibhrāntidarśanālabdha-bhūmikatvānavasthitatvāni
          cittavikṣepās te 'ntarāyāḥ iti/ tatra doṣatrayavaiṣamyanimitto jvarādir vyādhiḥ/
          cittasyākarmaṇyatvaṃ styānam/ viruddhakoṭidvayāvagāhi jñānaṃ saṃśayaḥ/ samādhisādhanānām
          abhāvanaṃ pramādaḥ/ śarīravākcittagurutvād apravṛttir ālasyam/ viṣayābhilāṣo 'viratiḥ/
          atasmiṃs tadbuddhir bhrāntidarśanam/ kutaścin nimittāt samādhibhūmer alābho
          'labdhabhūmikatvam/ labdhāyām api tasyām cittasyāpratiṣṭhānavasthitatvam ity arthaḥ/
          tasmān na vṛttinirodho yogapakṣanikṣepam arhatīti cet — maivaṃ vocaḥ/
          heyabhūtakṣiptādyavasthātraye vṛttinirodhasya yogatvāsaṃbhave 'py upādeyayor
          ekāgraniruddhāvasthayor vṛttinirodhasya yogatvasaṃbhavāt/ ekatānaṃ cittam ekāgram ucyate/
          niruddhasakalavṛttikaṃ saṃskāramātraśeṣaṃ cittaṃ niruddham iti bhaṇyate/ 
 [l. 15.239] 
 sa ca samādhir dvividhaḥ/ saṃprajñātāsaṃprajñātabhedāt/ tatraikāgracetasi yaḥ
          pramāṇādivṛttīnāṃ bāhyaviṣayāṇāṃ nirodhaḥ sa saṃprajñātaḥ samādhiḥ/ samyak prajñāyate
          'smin prakṛter viviktatayā dhyeyam iti vyutpatteḥ/ sa caturvidhaḥ/ savitarkādibhedāt/
          samādhir nāma bhāvanā/ sā ca bhāvyasya viṣayāntaraparihāreṇa cetasi punaḥ punar niveśanam/
          bhāvyaṃ ca dvividham — īśvaras tattvāni ca/ tāny api dvividhāni jaḍājaḍabhedāt/ jaḍāni
          prakṛtimahadahaṃkārādīni caturviṃśatiḥ/ ajaḍaḥ puruṣaḥ/ tatra yadā pṛthivyādīni sthūlāni
          viṣayatvenādāya pūrvāparānusaṃdhānena śabdārthollekhasaṃbhedena ca bhāvanā pravartate sa
          samādhiḥ savitarkaḥ/ yadā tanmātrāntaḥkaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ viṣayam ālambya
          deśādyavacchedena bhāvanā pravartate tadā savicāraḥ/ yadā rajastamoleśānuviddhaṃ cittaṃ
          bhāvyate tadā sukhaprakāśamayasya sattvasyodrekāt sānandaḥ/ yadā rajastamoleśānabhibhūtaṃ
          śuddhaṃ sattvam ālambanīkṛtya yā pravartate bhāvanā tadā tasyāṃ sattvasya nyagbhāvāc
          citiśakter udrekāc ca sattāmātrāvaśeṣatvena sāsmitaḥ samādhiḥ/ tad uktaṃ patañjalinā —
          vitarkavicārānandāsmitārūpānugamāt saṃprajñātaḥ iti/ sarvavṛttinirodhe tv asaṃprajñātaḥ
          samādhiḥ/ nanu sarvavṛttinirodho yoga ity ukte saṃprajñāte vyāptir na syāt/ tatra
          sattvapradhānāyāḥ sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātilakṣaṇāyā vṛtter anirodhād iti cet — tad etad
          vārtam/ kleśakarmavipākāśayaparipanthicittavṛttinirodho yoga ity aṅgīkārāt/ 
 [l. 15.260] 
 kleśāḥ punaḥ pañcadhā prasiddhā avidyāsmitārāgadveṣābhiniveśāḥ kleśāḥ iti/ 
 [l. 15.262] 
 nanv avidyety atra kim āśrīyate pūrvapadārthaprādhānyam amakṣikaṃ vartata itivat/
          uttarapadārthaprādhānyaṃ vā rājapuruṣa itivat/ 
 itivat/  ] ASS;  itivat  IV, A. 
  anyapadārthaprādhānyaṃ vā amakṣiko deśa itivat/ tatra na pūrvaḥ/
          pūrvapadārthaprādhānye avidyāyāṃ prasajyapratiṣedhopapattau kleśādikārakatvānupapatteḥ/
          avidyāśabdasya strīliṅgatvābhāvāpatteś ca/ na dvitīyaḥ/ kasyacid abhāvena viśiṣṭāyā
          vidyāyāḥ kleśādiparipanthitvena tadbījatvānupapatteḥ/ na tṛtīyaḥ/ naño 'styarthānāṃ
          bahuvrīhir vā cottarapadalopaś ceti vṛttikāravacanānusāreṇāvidyamānā vidyā yasyāḥ sā
          avidyā buddhir iti samāsārthasiddhau tasyā avidyāyāḥ kleśādibījatvānupapatteḥ/
          vivekakhyātipūrvakasarvavṛttinirodhasaṃpannāyās tasyās tathātvaprasaṅgāc ca/ uktaṃ
          cāsmitādīnāṃ kleśānām avidyānidānatvam — avidyā kṣetram 
 avidyā kṣetram° ] ASS; 
 avidyākṣetram° A, avidyā kṣetratvam° IV . 
  uttareṣāṃ prasuptatanuvicchinnodārāṇām iti/ tatra prasuptatvaṃ
          prabodhasahakāryabhāvenānabhivyaktiḥ/ tanutvaṃ pratipakṣabhāvanayā śithilīkaraṇam/
          vicchinnatvaṃ balavatā kleśenābhibhavaḥ/ udāratvaṃ sahakārisaṃnidhivaśāt kāryakāritvam/
          tad uktaṃ vācaspatimiśreṇa vyāsabhāṣyavyākhyāyām — 
 
 prasuptās tattvalīnānāṃ tanvavasthāś ca yoginām/ 
 vicchinnodārarūpāś ca kleśā viṣayasaṅginām// iti/ 
 
 dvandvavat svatantrapadārthadvayānavagamād ubhayapadārthapradhānatvaṃ nāśaṅkitam/ tasmāt
          pakṣatraye 'pi kleśādinidānatvam avidyāyāḥ prasiddhaṃ hīyeteti cet — 
 [l. 15.282] 
 tad api na śobhanaṃ vibhāti/ paryudāsaśaktim āśrityāvidyāśabdena vidyāviruddhasya
          viparyayajñānasyābhidhānam iti vṛddhair aṅgīkārāt/ tad āha — 
 
 nāmadhātvarthayoge tu naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥ/ 
 vadaty abrāhmaṇādharmāv anyamātravirodhinau// iti/ 
 vṛddhaprayogagamyo hi śabdārthaḥ sarva eva naḥ/ 
 tena yatra prayukto yo na tasmād apanīyate// iti/ 
 
 vācaspatimiśrair apy uktaṃ lokādhīnāvadhāraṇo hi śabdārthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ/ loke
          cottarapadārthapradhānasyāpi naña uttarapadābhidheyopamardakasya tadviruddhatayā tatra
          tatropalabdher ihāpi tadviruddhe pravṛttir iti/ 
 [l. 15.292] 
 etad evābhipretyoktam — anityāśuciduḥkhānātmasu nityaśucisukhātmakhyātir avidyā iti/
          atasmiṃs tadbuddhir viparyaya ity uktaṃ bhavati/ tad yathā — anitye ghaṭādau
          nityatvābhimānaḥ/ aśucau kāyādau śucitvapratyayaḥ — 
 
 sthānād bījād upaṣṭambhān niṣyandān nidhanād api/ 
 kāyam ādheyaśaucatvāt paṇḍitā hy aśuciṃ viduḥ// iti/ 
 
 pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhair guṇavṛttivirodhāc 
 ° guṇavṛttivirodhāc° ] IV;  ° guṇavṛttyavirodhāc° A . Vijñānabhikṣu's  Yogavārttika  has (and defends) the reading ° guṇavṛttyavirodhāc° . 
  ca duḥkham eva sarvaṃ vivekinaḥ iti nyāyena duḥkhe srakcandanavanitādau
          sukhatvāropaḥ/ anātmani dehādāv ātmabuddhiḥ/ tad uktam — 
 
 anātmani ca dehādāv ātmabuddhis tu dehinām/ 
 avidyā tatkṛto bandhas tannāśo mokṣa ucyate// iti/ 
 
 evam iyam avidyā catuṣpadā bhavati/ nanv eteṣv avidyāviśeṣeṣu kiṃcid anugataṃ
          sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ varṇanīyam/ anyathā viśeṣasyāsiddheḥ/ tathā coktaṃ bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ — 
 
 sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ muktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇam/ 
 na śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktum ato 'py asya na vācyatā// iti/ 
 
 tad api na vācyam/ atasmiṃs tadbuddhir iti sāmānyalakṣaṇābhidhānena dattottaratvāt/ 
 [l. 15.310] 
 sattvapuruṣayor aham asmīty ekatābhimāno 'smitā/ tad apy uktaṃ — dṛgdarśanaśaktyor
          ekātmatevāsmitā iti/ 
 [l. 15.312] 
 sukhābhijñasya sukhānusmṛtipūrvakaḥ sukhasādhaneṣu tṛṣṇārūpo gardho rāgaḥ/
          duḥkhābhijñasya tadanusmṛtipurassaraṃ tatsādhaneṣu nivṛttir dveṣaḥ/ tad uktaṃ —
          sukhānuśayī rāgaḥ duḥkhānuśayī dveṣaḥ iti/ 
 [l. 15.316] 
 kim atrānuśayiśabde tācchīlyārthe ṇinir inir vā matvarthīyo 'bhimataḥ/ nādyaḥ/ supy
          ajātau ṇinis tācchīlye ity atra supīti vartamāne punaḥ
          subgrahaṇasyopasarganivṛttyarthatvena sopasargād dhātor ṇiner anutpatteḥ/ yathākathaṃcit
          tadaṅgīkāre 'py aco ñṇiti iti vṛddhiprasaktāv atiśāyyādipadavad anuśāyipadasya
          prayogaprasaṅgāt/ na dvitīyaḥ/ 
 
 ekākṣarāt kṛto jāteḥ saptamyāṃ ca na tau smṛtau/ 
 
 iti tatpratiṣedhāt/ atra cānuśayaśabdasyājantatvena kṛdantatvāt/ tasmād anuśayiśabdo
          durupapāda iti cet — naitad bhadram/ bhāvānavabodhāt/ prāyikābhiprāyam idaṃ vacanam/ ata
          evoktaṃ vṛttikāreṇa — itikaraṇo vivakṣārthaḥ sarvatrābhisaṃbadhyate iti/ tena kvacid
          bhavati kāryī kāryikas taṇḍulī taṇḍulika iti/ tathā ca kṛdantāj jāteś ca pratiṣedhasya
          prāyikatvam/ anuśayaśabdasya kṛdantatayener upapattir iti siddham/ 
 [l. 15.330] 
 pūrvajanmānubhūtamaraṇaduḥkhānubhavavāsanābalāt sarvasya prāṇabhṛnmātrasyā kṛmer ā ca
          viduṣaḥ saṃjāyamānaḥ śarīraviṣayāder mama viyogo mā bhūd iti pratyahaṃ nimittaṃ vinā
          pravartamāno bhayarūpo 'bhiniveśaḥ pañcamaḥ kleśaḥ/ mā na bhūvaṃ hi bhūyāsaṃ iti
          prārthanāyāḥ pratyātmam anubhavasiddhatvāt/ tad āha — svarasavāhī viduṣo 'pi tathā rūḍho
          'bhiniveśaḥ iti/ 
 te cāvidyādayaḥ pañca sāṃsārikavividhaduḥkhopahārahetutvena puruṣaṃ kliśnantīti kleśāḥ
          prasiddhāḥ/ 
 [l. 15.337] 
 karmāṇi vihitapratiṣiddharūpāṇi jyotiṣṭomabrahmahatyādīni/ vipākāḥ karmaphalāni
          jātyāyurbhogāḥ/ ā phalavipākāc cittabhūmau śerata ity āśayā dharmādharmasaṃskārāḥ/ 
 tatparipanthicittavṛttinirodho yogaḥ/ nirodho nābhāvamātram abhimatam/ tasya tucchatvena
          bhāvarūpasākṣātkārajananakṣamatvāsaṃbhavāt/ kiṃ tu tadāśrayo
          madhumatīmadhupratīkāviśokāsaṃskāraśeṣāvyapadeśyaś cittasyāvasthāviśeṣaḥ/ nirudhyante
          'smin pramāṇādyāś cittavṛtaya iti vyutpatter upapatteḥ/ 
 [l. 15.343] 
 abhyāsavairāgyābhyāṃ vṛttinirodhaḥ/ tatra sthitau yatno 'bhyāsaḥ/ vṛttirahitasya cittasya
          svarūpaniṣṭhaḥ praśāntavāhitārūpaḥ pariṇāmaviśeṣaḥ sthitiḥ/ taṃ nimittīkṛtya yatnaḥ punaḥ
          punas tathātvena cetasi niveśanam abhyāsaḥ/ carmaṇi dvīpinam hantītivan nimittārtheyaṃ
          saptamīty uktaṃ bhavati/ dṛṣṭānuśravikaviṣayavitṛṣṇasya vaśīkārasaṃjñā vairāgyam/
          aihikapāratrikaviṣayādau doṣadarśanān nirabhilāṣasya mamaite viṣayā vaśyā nāham eteṣāṃ
          vaśya iti vimarśo vairāgyam ity uktaṃ bhavati/ 
 [l. 15.352] 
 samādhiparipanthikleśatanūkaraṇārthaṃ samādhilābhārthaṃ ca prathamaṃ
          kriyāyogavidhānapareṇa yoginā bhavitavyam/ kriyāyogasaṃpādane 'bhyāsavairāgyayoḥ
          saṃbhavāt/ tad uktaṃ bhagavatā — 
 
 ārurukṣor muner yogaṃ karma kāraṇam ucyate/ 
 yogārūḍhasya tasyaiva śamaḥ kāraṇam ucyate// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.357] 
 kriyāyogaś copadiṣṭaḥ patañjalinā — tapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni kriyāyogaḥ iti/
          tapaḥsvarūpaṃ nirūpitaṃ yājñavalkyena — 
 
 vidhinoktena mārgeṇa kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ/ 
 śarīraśoṣaṇaṃ prāhus tapasāṃ tapa uttamam// iti/ 
 
 praṇavagāyatrīprabhṛtīnāṃ mantrāṇām adhyayanaṃ svādhyāyaḥ/ 
 [l. 15.363] 
 te ca mantrā dvividhā vaidikās tāntrikāś ca/ vaidikāś ca dvividhāḥ pragītā apragītāś ca/
          tatra pragītāḥ sāmāni/ apragītāś ca dvividhāḥ/ chandobaddhās tadvilakṣaṇāś ca/ tatra
          prathamā ṛco dvitīyā yajūṃṣi/ tad uktaṃ jaimininā — teṣām ṛg yatrārthavaśena
          pādavyavasthā/ gītiṣu sāmākhyā/ śeṣe yajuḥśabdaḥ iti/ tantreṣu
          kāmikakāraṇaprapañcādyāgameṣu ye ye varṇitās te tāntrikāḥ/ te punar mantrās trividhāḥ
          strīpuṃnapuṃsakabhedāt/ tad āha — 
 
 strīpuṃnapuṃsakatvena trividhā mantrajātayaḥ/ 
 strīmantrā vahnijāyāntā namontāḥ syur napuṃsakāḥ// 
 śeṣāḥ pumāṃsas te śastāḥ siddhā vaśyādikarmaṇi/ iti/ 
 
 jananādisaṃskārābhāve 'pi nirastasamastadoṣatvena siddhihetutvāt siddhatvam/ 
 [l. 15.374] 
 sa ca saṃskāro daśavidhaḥ kathitaḥ śāradātilake — 
 
 mantrāṇāṃ daśa kathyante saṃskārāḥ siddhidāyinaḥ/ 
 nirdoṣatāṃ prayānty āśu te mantrāḥ sādhu saṃskṛtāḥ// 
 jananaṃ jīvanaṃ caiva tāḍanaṃ bodhanaṃ tathā/ 
 abhiṣeko 'tha vimalīkaraṇāpyāyane punaḥ/ 
 tarpaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ guptir daśaitā mantrasaṃskriyāḥ/ 
 mantrāṇāṃ mātṛkāyantrād uddhāro jananaṃ smṛtam// 
 praṇavāntaritān kṛtvā mantravarṇāñ japet sudhīḥ/ 
 mantrārṇasaṃkhyayā tad dhi jīvanaṃ saṃpracakṣate// 
 mantravarṇān samālikhya tāḍayec candanāmbhasā/ 
 
 [l. 15.384] 
 
 pratyekaṃ vāyubījena tāḍanaṃ tad udāhṛtam// 
 vilikhya mantravarṇāṃs tu prasūnaiḥ karavīrajaiḥ/ 
 tanmantrākṣarasaṃkhyātair 
 tanmantrākṣarasaṃkhyātair  ]  Śāradātilaka ;  mantrākṣareṇa 
 saṃkhyātair  A. 
  hanyāt tad bodhanaṃ matam// 
 svatantroktavidhānena mantrī mantrārṇasaṃkhyayā/ 
 aśvatthapallavair mantram abhiṣiñced viśuddhaye// 
 saṃcintya manasā mantraṃ jyotir mantreṇa nirdahet/ 
 mantre malatrayaṃ mantrī vimalīkaraṇaṃ hi tat// 
 tāravyomāgnimanuyug jyotir mantra udāhṛtaḥ/ 
 kuśodakena japtena pratyarṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥ// 
 vāribījena vidhivad etad āpyāyanaṃ matam/ 
 mantreṇa vāriṇā mantre tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ smṛtam// 
 tāramāyāramāyogo manor dīpanam ucyate/ 
 japyamānasya mantrasya gopanaṃ tv aprakāśanam// 
 saṃskārā daśa mantrāṇāṃ sarvatantreṣu gopitāḥ/ 
 yat kṛtvā saṃpradāyena mantrī vāñchitam aśnute// 
 ruddhakīlitavicchinnasuptaśaptādayo 'pi ca/ 
 mantradoṣāḥ praṇaśyanti saṃskārair ebhir uttamaiḥ// iti/ 
 
 tad alam akāṇḍatāṇḍavakalpena mantraśāstrarahasyodghoṣaṇena/ 
 [l. 15.402] 
 īśvarapraṇidhānaṃ nāmābhihitānām anabhihitānāṃ ca sarvāsāṃ kriyāṇāṃ parameśvare
          paramagurau phalānapekṣayā samarpaṇam/ yatredam uktam — 
 
 kāmato 'kāmato vāpi yat karomi śubhāśubham/ 
 tat sarvaṃ tvayi vinyastaṃ tvatprayuktaḥ karomy aham// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.407] 
 kriyāphalasaṃnyāso 'pi bhaktiviśeṣāparaparyāyaṃ praṇidhānam eva/ phalānabhisaṃdhānena
          karmakaraṇāt/ tathā ca gīyate gītāsu bhagavatā — 
 
 karmaṇy evādhikāras te mā phaleṣu kadācana/ 
 mā karmaphalahetur bhūr mā te saṅgo 'stv akarmaṇi// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.412] 
 phalābhisaṃdher upaghātakatvam abhihitaṃ bhagavadbhir nīlakaṇṭhabhāratīśrīcaraṇaiḥ — 
 
 api prayatnasaṃpannaṃ kāmenopahataṃ tapaḥ/ 
 na tuṣṭaye maheśasya śvalīḍham iva pāyasam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.416] 
 sā ca tapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānātmikā kriyā yogasādhanatvād yoga iti
          śuddhasāropalakṣaṇāvṛttyāśrayaṇena nirūpyate yathāyur ghṛtam iti/ 
 [l. 15.419] 
 śuddhasāropalakṣaṇā nāma lakṣaṇāprabhedaḥ/ mukhyārthabādhatadyogābhyām
          arthāntarapratipādanaṃ lakṣaṇā/ sā dvividhā/ rūḍhimūlā prayojanamūlā ca/ tad uktam
          kāvyaprakāśe — 
 
 mukhyārthabādhe tadyoge rūḍhito 'tha prayojanāt/ 
 anyo 'rtho lakṣyate yat sā lakṣaṇāropitā kriyā// iti/ 
 
 yacchabdena lakṣyata ity ākhyāte guṇībhūtaṃ pratipādanamātraṃ parāmṛśyate/ sā lakṣaṇeti
          pratinirdiśyamānāpekṣayā tacchabdasya strīliṅgatopapattiḥ/ tad uktaṃ kaiyaṭaiḥ —
          nirdiśyamānapratinirdiśyamānayor aikyam āpādayanti sarvanāmāni paryāyeṇa tattalliṅgam
          upādadata iti/ tatra karmaṇi kuśala ityādi rūḍhilakṣaṇāyā udāharaṇam/ kuśāṃl lātīti
          vyutpattyā darbhādānakartari yaugikaṃ kuśalapadaṃ vivecakatvasārūpyāt pravīṇe
          pravartamānam anādivṛddhavyavahāraparamparānupātitvenābhidhānavat prayojanam anapekṣya
          pravartate/ tad āha — 
 
 nirūḍhā lakṣaṇāḥ kāścit sāmarthyād abhidhānavat/ iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.435] 
 tasmād rūḍhilakṣaṇāyāḥ prayojanāpekṣā nāsti/ yady api prayuktaḥ śabdaḥ prathamaṃ
          mukhyārthaṃ pratipādayati tenārthenārthāntaraṃ lakṣyata ity arthadharmo 'yaṃ lakṣaṇā
          tathāpi tatpratipādake śabde samāropitaḥ sañ śabdavyāpāra iti vyapadiśyate/ etad
          evābhipretyoktaṃ lakṣaṇāropitā kriyeti/ prayojanalakṣaṇā tu ṣaḍvidhā/ upadānalakṣaṇā
          lakṣaṇalakṣaṇā gauṇasāropā gauṇasādhyavasānā śuddhasāropā śuddhasādhyavasānā ceti/ kuntāḥ
          praviśanti mañcāḥ krośanti gaur vāhīkaḥ gaur ayam āyur ghṛtam āyur evedam — iti
          yathākramam udāharaṇāni draṣṭavyāni/ tad uktam — 
 
 svasiddhaye parākṣepaḥ parārthaṃ svasamarpaṇam/ 
 upādānaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cety uktā śuddhaiva sā dvidhā// 
 sāropānyā tu yatroktau viṣayī viṣayas tathā/ 
 viṣayyantaḥkṛte 'nyasmin sā syāt sādhyavasānikā// 
 bhedāv imau ca sādṛśyāt saṃbandhāntaratas tathā/ 
 gauṇau śudhau ca vijñeyau lakṣaṇā tena ṣaḍvidhā// iti/ 
 
 tad alaṃ kāvyamīmāṃsāmarmanirmanthanena/ 
 [l. 15.451] 
 sa ca yogo yamādibhedavaśād aṣṭāṅga iti nirdiṣṭaḥ/ tatra yamā ahiṃsādayaḥ/ tad āha
          patañjaliḥ — ahiṃsāsatyāsteyabrahmacaryāparigrahā yamāḥ/ iti/ niyamāḥ śaucādayaḥ/ tad apy
          āha — śaucasaṃtoṣatapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni niyamāḥ iti/ ete ca yamaniyamā
          viṣṇupurāṇe darśitāḥ — 
 
 brahmacaryam ahiṃsāṃ ca satyāsteyāparigrahān/ 
 seveta yogī niṣkāmo yogyatāṃ svaṃ mano nayan// 
 svādhyāyaśaucasaṃtoṣatapāṃsi niyatātmavān/ 
 kurvīta brahmaṇi tathā parasmin pravaṇaṃ manaḥ// 
 ete yamāḥ saniyamāḥ pañca pañca prakīrtitāḥ/ 
 viśiṣṭaphaladāḥ kāme niṣkāmāṇāṃ vimuktidāḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.463] 
 sthirasukham āsanaṃ
          padmāsanabhadrāsanavīrāsanasvastikāsanadaṇḍakāsanasopāśrayaparyaṅka-krauñcaniṣadanoṣṭraniṣadanasamasaṃsthānabhedād
          daśavidham/ 
 
 pādāṅguṣṭhau nibadhnīyād dhastābhyāṃ vyutkrameṇa tu/ 
 ūrvor upari viprendra kṛtvā pādatale ubhe// 
 padmāsanaṃ bhaved etat sarveṣām abhipūjitam/ 
 
 ityādinā yājñavalkyaḥ padmāsanādisvarūpaṃ nirūpitavān/ tat sarvaṃ tata
          evāvagantavyam/ 
 tasminn āsanasthairye sati prāṇāyāmaḥ pratiṣṭhito bhavati/ sa ca śvāsapraśvāsayor
          gativicchedasvarūpaḥ/ tatra śvāso nāma bāhyasya vāyor antarānayanam/ praśvāsaḥ punaḥ
          koṣṭhyasya bahirniḥsāraṇam/ tayor ubhayor api saṃcaraṇābhāvaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ/ nanu nedaṃ
          prāṇāyāmasāmānyalakṣaṇam/ tadviśeṣeṣu recakapūrakakumbhakaprakāreṣu tadanugater ayogād iti
          cet — naiṣa doṣaḥ/ sarvatrāpi śvāsapraśvāsagativicchedasaṃbhavāt/ tathā hi/ koṣṭhyasya
          vāyor bahirniḥsaraṇaṃ recekaḥ prāṇāyāmo yaḥ praśvāsatvena prāg uktaḥ/ bāhyasya vāyor
          antardhāraṇaṃ pūrako yaḥ śvāsarūpaḥ/ antaḥstambhavṛttiḥ kumbhakaḥ/ yasmiñ jalam iva kumbhe
          niścalatayā prāṇākhyo vāyur avasthāpyate/ tatra sarvatra śvāsapraśvāsadvayagativicchedo
          'sty eveti nāsti śaṅkāvakāśaḥ/ tad uktaṃ tasmin sati śvāsapraśvāsayor gativicchedaḥ
          prāṇāyāmaḥ iti/ 
 [l. 15.482] 
 sa ca vāyuḥ sūryodayam ārabhya sārdhaghaṭikādvayaṃ
          ghaṭīyantrasthitaghaṭabhramaṇanyāyenaikasyāṃ nāḍyāṃ bhavati/ evaṃ saty aharniśaṃ
          śvāsapraśvāsayoḥ ṣaṭśatādhikaikaviṃśatisahasrāṇi jāyante/ ata evoktaṃ
          mantrasamarpaṇarahasyavedibhir ajapāmantrasamarpaṇe — 
 
 ṣaṭśatāni gaṇeśāya ṣaṭsahasraṃ svayaṃbhuve/ 
 viṣṇave ṣaṭsahasraṃ ca ṣaṭsahasraṃ pinākine// 
 sahasram ekaṃ gurave sahasraṃ paramātmane/ 
 sahasram ātmane caivam arpayāmi kṛtaṃ japam// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.490] 
 tathā nāḍīsaṃcāraṇadaśāyāṃ vāyoḥ saṃcaraṇe pṛthivyādīni tattvāni varṇaviśeṣavaśāt
          puruṣārthābhilāṣukaiḥ puruṣair avagantavyāni/ tad uktam abhiyuktaiḥ — 
 
 sārdhaṃ ghaṭīdvayaṃ nāḍyor ekaikārkodayād vahet/ 
 araghaṭṭaghaṭībhrāntinyāyo nāḍyoḥ punaḥ punaḥ// 
 śatāni tatra jāyante niśvāsocchvāsayor nava/ 
 khakhaṣaṭkadvikaiḥ saṃkhyāhorātre sakale punaḥ// 
 ṣaṭtriṃśadguruvarṇānāṃ yā velā bhaṇane bhavet/ 
 sā velā maruto nāḍyantare saṃcarato bhavet// 
 pratyekaṃ pañca tattvāni nāḍyoś ca vahamānayoḥ/ 
 vahanty aharniśaṃ tāni jñātavyāni yatātmabhiḥ// 
 ūrdhvaṃ vahnir adhas toyaṃ tiraścīnaḥ samīraṇaḥ/ 
 bhūmim ardhapuṭe vyoma sarvagaṃ pravahet punaḥ// 
 vāyor vahner apāṃ pṛthvyā vyomnas tattvaṃ vahet kramāt/ 
 vahantyor ubhayor nāḍyor jñātavyo 'yam kramaḥ sadā// 
 pṛthvyāḥ palāni pañcāśac catvāriṃśat tathāmbhasaḥ/ 
 agnes triṃśat punar vāyor viṃśatir nabhaso daśa// 
 pravāhakālasaṃkhyeyaṃ hetus tatra pradarśyate/ 
 pṛthvī pañcaguṇā toyaṃ caturguṇam athānalaḥ// 
 triguṇo dviguṇo vāyur viyad ekaguṇaṃ bhavet/ 
 guṇaṃ prati daśa palāny urvyāṃ pañcāśad ity ataḥ// 
 ekaikahānis toyādes tathā pañca guṇāḥ kṣiteḥ/ 
 gandho rasaś ca rūpaṃ ca sparśaḥ śabdaḥ kramād amī// 
 tattvābhyāṃ bhūjalābhyāṃ syāc chāntiḥ kārye phalonnatiḥ/ 
 dīptāsthirāvyūhavṛttis tejovāyvambareṣu ca// 
 pṛthvyaptejomarudvyomatattvānāṃ cihnam ucyate/ 
 ādye sthairyaṃ svacittasya śaitye kāmodbhavo bhavet// 
 tṛtīye kopasaṃtāpau caturthe cañcalātmatā/ 
 pañcame śūnyataiva syād atha vādharmavāsanā// 
 śrutyor aṅguṣṭhakau madhyāṅgulyau nāsāpuṭadvaye/ 
 sṛkkiṇyoḥ prāntyakopāntyāṅgulī śeṣe dṛgantayoḥ// 
 nyasyāntaḥsthapṛthivyāditattvajñānaṃ bhavet kramāt/ 
 pītaśvetāruṇaśyāmair bindubhir nirupādhi kham// ityādinā/ 
 
 [l. 15.523] 
 yathāvad vāyutattvam avagamya tanniyamane vidhīyamāne vivekajñānāvaraṇakarmakṣayo
          bhavati/ tapo na paraṃ prāṇāyāmād iti/ 
 
 dahyante dhmāyamānānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hi yathā malāḥ/ 
 prāṇāyāmais tu dahyante tadvad indriyajā malāḥ// iti ca/ 
 
 [l. 15.527] 
 tad evaṃ yamādibhiḥ saṃskṛtamanaskasya yoginaḥ saṃyamāya pratyāhāraḥ kartavyaḥ/
          cakṣurādīnām indriyāṇāṃ
          pratiniyatarañjanīyakopanīyamohanīyapravaṇatvaprahāṇenāvikṛtasvarūpa-pravaṇacittānukāraḥ
          pratyāhāraḥ/ indriyāṇi viṣayebhyaḥ pratīpam āhriyante 'sminn iti vyutpatteḥ/ nanu tadā
          cittam abhiniviśate nendriyāṇi/ teṣāṃ bāhyaviṣayatvena tatra sāmarthyābhāvāt/ ataḥ kathaṃ
          cittānukāraḥ/ addhā/ ata eva vastutas tasyāsaṃbhavam abhisaṃdhāya sādṛśyārtham ivaśabdaṃ
          cakāra sūtrakāraḥ — svaviṣayāsaṃprayoge cittasvarūpānukāra ivendriyāṇāṃ pratyāhāraḥ iti/
          sādṛśyaṃ ca cittānukāranimittaṃ viṣayāsaṃprayogaḥ/ yadā cittaṃ nirudhyate tadā
          cakṣurādīnāṃ nirodhe prayatnāntaraṃ nāpekṣaṇīyam/ yathā madhukararājaṃ madhumakṣikā
          anuvartate tathendriyāṇi cittam iti/ tad uktaṃ viṣṇupūrāṇe — 
 
 śabdādiṣv anuraktāni nigṛhyākṣāṇi yogavit/ 
 kuryāc cittānukārīṇi pratyāhāraparāyaṇaḥ// 
 vaśyatā paramā tena jāyate 'ticalātmanām/ 
 indriyāṇām avaśyais tair na yogī yogasādhakaḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.544] 
 nābhicakrahṛdayapuṇḍarīkanāsāgrādāv ādhyātmike hiraṇyagarbhavāsavaprajāpatiprabhṛtike
          bāhye vā deśe cittasya viṣayāntaraparihāreṇa sthirīkaraṇaṃ dhāraṇā/ tad āha — deśabandhaś
          cittasya dhāraṇā iti/ paurāṇikāś ca — 
 
 prāṇāyāmena pavanaṃ pratyāhāreṇa cendriyam/ 
 vaśīkṛtya tataḥ kuryāc cittasthānaṃ śubhāśraye// iti/ 
 
 [l. 15.551] 
 tasmin deśe dhyeyāvalambanasya pratyayasya visadṛśapratyayaprahāṇena pravāho dhyānam/ tad
          uktaṃ — tatra pratyayaikatānatā dhyānam iti/ anyair apy uktam — 
 
 tadrūpapratyayaikāgryā saṃtatiś cānyaniḥspṛhā// 
 tad dhyānaṃ prathamair aṅgaiḥ ṣaḍbhir niṣpādyate nṛpa// iti/ 
 
 prasaṅgāc caramam aṅgaṃ prāg eva pratyapīpadāma/ 
 [l. 15.558] 
 tad anena yogāṅgānuṣṭhānenādaranairantaryadīrghakālasevitena
          samādhipratipakṣakleśaprakṣaye 'bhyāsavairāgyavaśān madhumatyādisiddhilābho bhavati/ 
 [l. 15.560] 
 atha kim evam akasmād asmān ativikaṭābhir atyantāprasiddhābhiḥ karṇāṭagauḍalāṭabhāṣābhir
          bhīṣayate bhavān/ na hi vayaṃ bhavantaṃ bhīṣayāmahe/ kiṃ tu
          madhumatyādipadārthavyutpādanena toṣayāmaḥ/ tataś cākutobhayena bhavatā śrūyatām
          avadhānena/ 
 tatra madhumatī nāmābhyāsavairāgyādivaśād
          apāstarajastamoleśasukhaprakāśamayasattvabhāvanayānavadyavaiśāradyavidyotanarūpaṛtaṃbharaprajñākhyā
          samādhisiddhiḥ/ tad uktam ṛtaṃbharā tatra prajñā iti/ ṛtaṃ satyaṃ bibharti kadācid api na
          viparyayeṇācchādyate/ tatra sthitau dārḍhye sati dvitīyasya yoginaḥ sā prajñā bhavatīty
          arthaḥ/ 
 catvāraḥ khalu yoginaḥ prasiddhāḥ prāthamakalpiko madhubhūmikaḥ prajñājyotir
          atikrāntabhāvanīyaś ceti/ tatrābhyāsī pravṛttamātrajyotiḥ prathamaḥ/ na tv anena
          paracittādigocarajñānarūpaṃ jyotir vaśīkṛtam ity uktaṃ bhavati/ ṛtaṃbharaprajño dvitīyaḥ/
          bhūtendriyajayī tṛtīyaḥ/ paravairāgyasaṃpannaś caturthaḥ/ 
 manojavitvādayo madhupratīkasiddhayaḥ/ tad uktaṃ — manojavitvaṃ vikaraṇabhāvaḥ
          pradhānajayaś ca iti/ manojavitvaṃ nāma kāyasya manovad anuttamo gatilābhaḥ/
          vikaraṇabhāvaḥ kāyanirapekṣāṇām indriyāṇām abhimatadeśakālaviṣayāpekṣavṛttilābhaḥ/
          pradhānajayaḥ prakṛtivikāreṣu sarveṣu vaśitvam/ etāś ca siddhayaḥ karaṇapañcakarūpajayāt
          tṛtīyasya yoginaḥ prādurbhavanti/ yathā madhuna ekadeśo 'pi svadate tathā pratyekam eva
          tāḥ siddhayaḥ svadanta iti madhupratīkāḥ/ sarvabhāvādhiṣṭhātṛtvādirūpā viśokā siddhiḥ/ tad
          āha — sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātimātrasya sarvabhāvādhiṣṭhātṛtvaṃ sarvajñatvaṃ ca iti/
          sarveṣāṃ vyavasāyāvyavasāyātmakānāṃ guṇapariṇāmarūpāṇāṃ bhāvanānāṃ svāmivad ākramaṇaṃ
          sarvabhāvādhiṣṭhātṛtvam/ teṣām eva śāntoditāvyapadeśyadharmitvena sthitānāṃ vivekajñānaṃ
          sarvajñātṛtvam/ tad uktaṃ — viśokā vā jyotiṣmatī iti/ sarvavṛttipratyastamaye paraṃ
          vairāgyam āśritya jātyādibījānāṃ kleśānāṃ nirodhasamartho nirbījaḥ samādhir
          asaṃprajñātapadavedanīyaḥ saṃskāraśeṣatāvyapadeśyaś cittasyāvasthāviśeṣaḥ/ tad uktaṃ —
          virāmapratyayābhyāsapūrvaḥ saṃskāraśeṣo 'nyaḥ iti/ evaṃ ca sarvato virajyamānasya tasya
          puruṣadhaureyasya kleśabījāni nirdagdhaśālibījakalpāni prasavasāmarthyavidhurāṇi manasā
          sārdhaṃ pratyastaṃ gacchanti/ 
 [l. 15.592] 
 tad eteṣu pralīneṣu nirupaplavavivekakhyātiparipākavaśāt kāryakāraṇātmakānāṃ pradhāne
          layaḥ citiśaktiḥ svarūpapratiṣṭhā punarbuddhisattvābhisaṃbandhavidhurā vā kaivalyaṃ
          labhata iti siddham/ 
 dvayī ca muktir uktā patañjalinā — puruṣārthaśūnyānāṃ guṇānāṃ pratiprasavaḥ kaivalyaṃ
          svarūpapratiṣṭhā vā citiśaktiḥ iti/ na cāsmin saty api kasmān na jāyate jantur iti
          vaditavyam/ kāraṇābhāvāt kāryābhāva iti pramāṇasiddhārthe niyogānuyogayor ayogāt/ aparathā
          kāraṇābhāve 'pi kāryasaṃbhave maṇivedhādayo 'ndhādibhyo bhaveyuḥ/ tathā
          cānupapannārthatāyām ābhāṇako laukika upapannārtho bhavet/ tathā ca śrutiḥ — andho maṇim
          avindat/ tam anaṅgulir āvayat/ agrīvaḥ pratyamuñcat/ tam ajihvā asaścata/ avindad
          avidhyata/ āvayat gṛhītavān/ pratyamuñcat pinaddhavān/ asaścatābhyapūjayat stutavān iti
          yāvat/ evaṃ ca cikitsāśāstravad yogaśāstraṃ caturvyūham/ yathā cikitsāśāstraṃ rogo
          rogahetur ārogyaṃ bheṣajam iti tathedam api saṃsāraḥ saṃsārahetur mokṣo mokṣopāya iti/
          tatra duḥkhamayaḥ saṃsāro heyaḥ/ pradhānapuruṣayoḥ saṃyogo heyabhogahetuḥ/ tasyātyantikī
          nivṛttir hānam/ tadupāyaḥ samyagdarśanam/ evam anyad api śāstraṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ
          caturvyūham ūhanīyaṃ iti sarvam avadātam/ (itaḥ paraṃ sarvadarśanaśiromaṇibhūtaṃ
          śāṃkaradarśanam anyatra likhitam ity atropekṣitam) 
 [l. 15.610] 
 iti sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe pātañjadarśanam// 
 
 
        [atha śāṃkaradarśanam //16//]

         [l. 16.1] 
 so ’yaṃ pariṇāmavādaḥ prāmāṇikagarhaṇam arhati/ na hy acetanaṃ pradhānaṃ
          cetanānadhiṣṭhitaṃ pravartate/ suvarṇādau rucakādyupādāne
          hemakārādicetanādhiṣṭhānopalambhena nityatvasādhakakṛtakatvavat/
          sukhaduḥkhamohātmanā'nvitatvādeḥ sādhanasya sādhyaviparyayavyāptatayā viruddhatvāt/
          svarūpasiddhatvāc ca/ āntarāḥ khalv amī sukhaduḥkhamohā bāhyebhyaś candanādibhyo
          vibhinnaprat thatyayavedanīyebhyo vyatiriktā adhyakṣam īkṣyante/ yady amī sukhādisvabhāvā
          bhaveyus tadā hemante ’pi candanaḥ sukhaḥ syāt/ na hi candanaḥ kadācid acandanaḥ/ tathā
          nidāgheṣv api kuṅkumapaṅkaḥ sukho bhavet/ na hy asau kadācid akuṅkumapaṅka iti/ evaṃ
          kaṇṭakaḥ kramelakasyeva manuṣyādīnām api prāṇabhṛtāṃ sukhaḥ syāt/ na hy asau kāṃścit praty
          eva kaṇṭaka iti/ tasmāc candanakuṅkumādayo viśeṣāḥ kālaviśeṣādyapekṣayā sukhādihetavo na
          tu sukhādisvabhāvā iti ramaṇīyam/ tasmād dhetur asiddha iti siddham/ 
 [l. 16.14] 
 nāpi śrutiḥ pradhānakāraṇatvavāde pramāṇam/ yataḥ: yad agne rohitaṃ rūpaṃ tejasas tad
          rūpaṃ yac chuklaṃ tad apām yat kṛṣṇaṃ tad annasya iti cchāndogyaśākhāyāṃ tejobannātmikāyāḥ
          prakṛter lohitaśuklakṛṣṇarūpāṇi samāmnātāni tāny evātra pratyabhijñāyante/ tatra
          śrautapratyabhijñāyāḥ prābalyāl lohitādiśabdānāṃ mukhyārthasaṃbhavāc ca tejobannātmikā
          jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjacatuṣṭayasya bhūtagrāmasya prakṛtir avasīyate/ yady api
          tejobannānāṃ prakṛter jātatvena yogavṛttyā na jāyata ity ajatvaṃ na sidhyati tathāpi
          rūḍhivṛttyāvagatam ajātatvam uktaprakṛtau sukhāvabodhāya prakalpyate/ yathā asau vādityo
          devamadhu ityādivākyenādityasya madhutvaṃ parikalpyate tathā tejobannātmikā prakṛtir
          evājeti/ ato ’jām ekām ityādikā śrutir api na pradhānapratipādikā/ 
 [l. 16.26] 
 yad avādi nidarśanaṃ pūrvavādinā kṣīrādikam acetanaṃ cetanānadhiṣṭhitam eva
          vatsavivṛddhyarthaṃ pravartata iti/ naitad ramaṇīyam/ buddhiviśeṣaśālinaḥ parameśvarasya
          tatrāpy adhiṣṭhātṛtvābhyupagamāt/ na ca parameśvarasya karuṇayā pravṛttyaṅgīkāre
          prāguktavikalpāvasaraḥ/ sṛṣṭeḥ prāk prāṇināṃ duḥkhasaṃbandhāsaṃbhave ’pi
          tannidānādṛṣṭasaṃbandhasaṃbhavena tatprahāṇecchayā pravṛttyupapatteḥ/ kiṃ ca
          puruṣārthaprayuktā pradhānapravṛttir ity uktaṃ tad vivektavyam/ kiṃ pradhānaṃ kevalaṃ
          bhogārthaṃ pravartate kiṃ vā kevalamokṣārtham āhosvid ubhayārtham/ na tāvad ādyaḥ kalpo
          ’vakalpate/ anādheyātiśayasya kūṭasthanityasya puruṣasya tāttvikabhogāsaṃbhavāt/
          anirmokṣaprasaṅgāc ca/ yena hi prayojanena pradhānaṃ pravartitaṃ tad anena vidhātavyam/
          bhogena caitat pravartitam iti tam eva vidadhyān na mokṣam iti/ nāpi dvitīyaḥ/ ciddhātor
          nityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvatayā karmānubhavavāsanānām asaṃbhavena pradhānapravṛtteḥ
          prāg api muktatayā tadarthaṃ pravṛttyanupapatteḥ/ śabdādyupabhogārtham apravṛttatvena
          pradhānasya tadajanakatvaprasaṅgāc ca/ nāpi tṛtīyaḥ/ prāguktadūṣaṇalaṅghanālaṅghitatvāt/
          pravṛttisvabhāvāyāḥ prakṛter audāsinyāyogāc ca/ 
 [l. 16.41] 
 nanu sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātiḥ puruṣārthaḥ/ tasyām jātāyāṃ sā nivartate kṛtakāryatvād iti
          cet 
 tad asamañjasam/ acetanāyāḥ prakṛter vicārya kāryakāritvāyogāt/ yatheyaṃ kṛte ’pi
          śabdādyupalambhe tadarthaṃ punaḥ pravartata evam atrāpi punaḥ pravarteta/
          svabhāvasyānapāyāt/ 
 [l. 16.45] 
 kiṃ ca sā prakṛtir vivekakhyātivaśād ucchidyate na vā/ ucchede sarvasya saṃprati saṃsāro
          ’stam iyāt/ anucchede na kasya cin mokṣaḥ/ 
 [l. 16.46] 
 nanu pradhānābhede ’pi tattatpuruṣāvivekakhyātilakṣaṇāvidyāsadasattvanibandhanau
          bandhamokṣāv upapadyeyātām iti cet 
 hanta tarhi kṛtaṃ prakṛtyā/ avidyāsadasadbhāvābhyām eva tadupapatteḥ/ 
 [l. 16.49] 
 nanv avidyāpakṣe ’py eṣa doṣaḥ prāduḥṣyād iti cet 
 tad etat pratyavasthānam asthāne/ na hi vayaṃ pradhānavad avidyāṃ sarveṣu jīveṣv ekām
          ācakṣmahe yenaivam upālabhyemahi/ api tv iyaṃ pratijīvaṃ bhidyate/ tena yasyaiva jīvasya
          vidyotpadyate tasyaivāvidyā samucchidyate nānyasya/ bhinnāyatanayos tayor virodhābhāvāt/
          ato na samastasaṃsārocchedaprasaṅgadoṣaḥ/ tasmāt pariṇāmaḥ parityaktavyaḥ/ svīkartavyaś ca
          vivartavādaḥ/ 
 [l. 16.55] 
 nanu jīvajaḍayoḥ sārūpyābhāvena cidvivartatvaṃ prapañcasya na saṃparipadyata iti prāg
          avādiṣmeti cet 
 naitat sādhu/ na hi sārūpyanibandhanāḥ sarve vibhramā iti vyāptir asti/ asarūpād api
          kāmādeḥ kāntāliṅganādiṣv iva svapnavibhramasyopalambhāt/ kiṃ ca kādācitke vibhrame
          sārūpyāpekṣā nānādyavidyānibandhane prapañce/ tad avocad ācāryavācaspatiḥ : 
 
 vivartas tu prapañco ’yaṃ brahmaṇo ’pariṇāminaḥ/ 
 anādivāsanodbhūto na sārūpyam apekṣate// iti/ 
 
 tad etat sarvaṃ vedāntaśāstrapariśramaśālināṃ sugamaṃ sughaṭaṃ ca/ 
 [l. 16.64] 
 tac ca vedāntaśāstraṃ caturlakṣaṇam/ bhagavatā bādarāyaṇena praṇītasya vedāntaśāstrasya
          pratyagbrahmaikyaṃ viṣaya iti śaṃkarācāryāḥ pratyapīpadan/ tatra prathame samanvayādhyāye
          sarveṣāṃ vedāntānāṃ brahmaṇi tātparyeṇa paryavasānam/ dvitīye ’virodhādhyāye
          sāṃkhyāditarkavirodhanirākaraṇam/ tṛtīye sādhanādhyāye brahmavidyāsādhanam/ caturthe
          phalādhyāye vidyāphalam/ tatra pratyadhyāyaṃ pādacatuṣṭayam/ tatra prathamasyādhyāyasya
          prathame pāde spaṣṭabrahmaliṅgaṃ vākyajātaṃ mīmāṃsyate/ dvitīye ’spaṣṭabrahmaliṅgam
          upāsyaviṣayam/ tṛtīye tādṛśaṃ jñeyaviṣayam/ caturthe ’vyaktājāpadādi saṃdigdhaṃ padajātam
          iti/ avirodhasya dvitīyasya prathame sāṃkhyayogakaṇādādismṛtivirodhaparihāraḥ/ dvitīye
          sāṃkhyādimatānāṃ duṣṭatvam/ tṛtīye pañcamahābhūtaśrutīnāṃ jīvaśrutīnāṃ ca
          parasparavirodhaparihāraḥ/ caturthe liṅgaśarīraśrutīnāṃ virodhaparihāraḥ/ 
 [l. 16.76] 
 tṛtīyasya prathame jīvasya paralokagamanāgamanavicārapuraḥsaraṃ vairāgyam/ dvitīye
          tvaṃpadatatpadārthapariśodhanam/ tṛtīye saguṇavidyāsu guṇopasaṃhāraḥ/ caturthe
          nirguṇabrahmavidyāyā bahiraṅgāntaraṅgāśramayajñaśamādisādhanajātam/ caturthasya prathame
          brahmasākṣātkāreṇa jīvataḥ pāpapuṇyakleśavaidhuryalakṣaṇā muktiḥ/ dvitīye
          maraṇotkramaṇaprakāraḥ/ tṛtīye saguṇabrahmopāsakasyottaramārgaḥ/ caturthe
          nirguṇasaguṇabrahmavido videhakaivalyabrahmalokāvasthānāni/ tad itthaṃ
          brahmavicāraśāstrādhyāyapādārthasaṃgrahaḥ/ 
 [l. 16.84] 
 tatra prathamam adhikaraṇam athāto brahmajijñāsā iti brahmamīmāṃsārambhopapādanaparam/
          adhikaraṇaṃ ca pañcāvayavaṃ prasiddham/ te ca viṣayādayaḥ pañcāvayavā nirūpyante/ ātmā vā are 
 ātmā vā are  ] ASS;  ātmā vāre  A. 
  draṣṭavyaḥ ity etad vākyaṃ viṣayaḥ/ brahma jijñāsitavyaṃ na veti saṃdehaḥ/
          jijñāsyatvavyāpakayoḥ saṃdehaprayojanayoḥ saṃbhavāsaṃbhavābhyām/ 
 [l. 16.90] 
 tatra kasyedaṃ jijñāsyatvam avagamyate/ ahamanubhavagamyasya śrutigamyasya vā/ 
 -nādyaḥ/ sarvajanīnenāhamanubhavenedamāspadadehādibhyo vivekenātmanaḥ spaṣṭaṃ
          pratibhāsamānatvāt/ 
 nanu sthūlo ’haṃ kṛśo ’ham ityādidehadharmasāmānādhikaraṇyānubhavād
          adhyastātmabhāvadehālambano ’yam ahaṃkāra iti cen na/ 
 bālyādyavasthāsu bhinnaparimāṇatayā badarāmalakādivat parasparabhedena śarīrasya
          pratyabhijñānānupapatteḥ/ 
 athocyeta yathā pīlupākapakṣe piṭharapākapakṣe vā kālabhedenaikasmin vastuni pākajabhedo
          yujyate tathaikasmiñ śarīrābhidhe vastuni kālabhedena parimāṇabhedaḥ/ ata eva laukikāḥ
          śarīram ātmanaḥ sakāśād abhinnaṃ pratipadyamānāḥ pratyabhijānate ceti/ 
 na tad bhadram/ maṇimantrauṣadhādyupāyabhedena bhūmikādhānavan nānāvidhān dehān
          pratipadyamānasyāhamālambanasya bhinnasyātmanaḥ śarīrād bhedena bhāsamānatvāt/ ata eva
          cakṣurādīnām apy ahamālambanatvam aśakyaśaṅkam/ nānyadṛṣṭam smaraty anyaḥ iti nyāyena
          cakṣurādau naṣṭe ’pi rūpādipratisaṃdhānānupapatteḥ/ nāpy antaḥkaraṇasyāhamālambanatvam
          āstheyam/ ayam eva bhedo bhedahetur vā yad viruddhadharmādhyāsaḥ kāraṇabhedaś ceti nyāyena
          kartṛkaraṇabhūtayor ātmāntaḥkaraṇayos takṣavāsivat saṃbhedāsaṃbhavāt/ yady abheda eva
          nādriyate tarhi sthūlo ’haṃ kṛśo ’haṃ kṛṣṇo ’ham ityādi saṃkhyānam utsannasaṃkathaṃ
          syāt/ 
 na syāt/ evaṃ loke śāstre cobhayathā śabdaprayogadarśanena mukhyārthatvānupapattau mañcāḥ
          krośantītyādivad aupacārikatvenopapatteḥ/ 
 -na dvitīyaḥ/ ahamanubhavagamyasyaiva śrutigamyatvāt/ satyaṃ jñānam anantaṃ brahma
          ityādiśrutibhyo hi brahmāvagamyate/ brahmabhāvaś cāham ātmā brahma tat tvam asi
          ityādiśrutiṣv ahaṃpratyayagamyasyaiva bodhyate/ tathā cedam anumānaṃ samasūci/ vimatam
          ajijñāsyam asaṃdigdhatvāt karatalāmalakavat/ 
 [l. 16.116] 
 tathā phalaṃ na phalabhāvam īkṣate/ puruṣair arthyata iti vyutpattyā
          niḥśeṣaduḥkhopaśamalakṣitaṃ paramānandaikarasaṃ ca puruṣārthaśabdasyārthaḥ
          sakalapuruṣadhaureyaiḥ prepsyate naitat sāṃsārikaṃ sukhajātam/ tasyaihikasya
          pāralaukikasya ca sātiśayatayā ca sadṛkṣatayā ca prekṣāvadbhir arthyamānatvānupapatteḥ/
          yat tatparipanthi duḥkhajātaṃ taj jihāsyate/ tac cāvidyāparaparyāyasaṃsāra eva/
          kartṛtvādisakalānarthakaratvād avidyāyāḥ/ sam ity ekīkaraṇe vartate/ saṃbhedādau tathā
          copalambhāt/ tathā cātmānaṃ dehenaikīkṛtya svarganarakamārgayoḥ sarati yena puruṣaḥ sa
          saṃsāro ’vidyāśabdārthaḥ/ tannivṛttiḥ phalaṃ phalavatām abhimatam/ tathā kathitam : 
 
 avidyāstamayo mokṣaḥ sā ca bandha udāhṛtaḥ/ iti 
 
 [l. 16.127] 
 tac ca kāśakuśāvalambanakalpam/ ātmayāthātmyānubhavena saha vartamānasya saṃsārasya
          rūparasavad virodhābhāvena nivartyanivartakabhāvābhāvāt/ 
 nanu sahānuvartamāno bodhaḥ saṃsāraṃ mā bādhiṣṭa/ sahāvartamānas tu bodhaḥ prakāśas
          tamovad bādhiṣyata iti cet 
 tad etad riktaṃ vacaḥ/ ahamanubhavād anyasyātmajñānasya mūṣikaviṣāṇāyamānatvāt/ 
 [l. 16.132] 
 nanv anyo ’yam anubhavaḥ pāmarāṇāṃ mā sma bhavan nāma/
          vedāntavacananicayaparyālocanakṣamāṇāṃ parīkṣakāṇāṃ saṃbhavaty evety api na vaktavyam/
          abādhitānubhavavirodhena vedāntavākyānāṃ grāvaplavanādivākyakalpatvāt/ na hy āgamāḥ
          paraḥśataṃ ghaṭaṃ paṭayitum utsahante/ na cādhyayanavidhivyākopaḥ/ gurumatānusāreṇa
          huṃphaḍādivākyavaj japamātropayogitvenācāryamatānusāreṇa vā yajamānaḥ prastara
          ityādivākyavat stāvakatvena vedāntasiddhāntasyādhyetavyatvasaṃbhavāt/ 
 tathā ca prayogaḥ : 
 vivādāspadaṃ brahma vicāryapadaṃ na bhavaty aphalatvāt kākadantavad iti/ tad āhur
          ācāryāḥ: 
 
 ahaṃdhiyātmanaḥ siddhes tasyaiva brahmabhāvataḥ/ 
 tajjñānān muktyabhāvāc ca jijñāsā nāvakalpate// iti/ 
 
 [l. 16.142] 
 na ca bhedenādhyastadehādinivṛttiḥ phalam ity aphalahetur asiddha iti veditavyam/
          bhedagraho hi vyāpakanivṛttyā vyāpyanivṛttir iti nyāyena bhedāgrahaparipathinaṃ
          bhedasaṃskāram apekṣate/ anākalitakaladhautasya śuktiśakale tatsamāropānupalambhāt/
          saṃskāraś ca pramitim ākāṅkṣati/ ananubhūte saṃskārānudayāt/ na ca bhrāntirūpo ’nubhavas
          tatkaraṇam iti bhaṇitavyam/ bhrānter abhrāntipūrvakatvena kvacit pramiter
          avaśyābhyupagamayitavyatvāt/ prayogaś ca: vimatāv ātmānātmānau bhedena pramitāv
          abhedāyogyatvāt/ tamaḥprakāśavat/ na cātmānātmanor abhedāyogyatvalakṣaṇo hetur asiddha iti
          śaṅkanīyam/ vikalpāsahatvāt/ tathā hi: anātmātmapariśeṣaḥ syād ātmānātmapariśeṣo vā/ ādye
          muktidaśāyām iva paridṛśyamānaṃ jagad astam iyāt/ dvitīye jagadāndhyaṃ prasajyeta/
          tamaḥprakāśavad viruddhasvabhāvatvāc ca dṛgdṛśyayor ātmānātmanor abhedāyogyatvam
          avadheyam/ tataś cārthādhyāsānupapattau tatpūrvakasya jñānādhyāsasyāsaṃbhavena brahmaṇo
          vicāryatvāsaṃbhavād vicārātmikā caturlakṣaṇaśārīrakamīmāṃsā nārambhaṇīyeti pūrvapakṣe
          prāpte siddhānto ’bhidhīyate/ 
 [l. 16.158] 
 ahaṃpadādhigamyād anyad ātmatattvaṃ nāstīti na vaktavyam/
          nirastasamastopādhikasyātmatattvasya śrutyādiṣu prasiddhatvāt/ na ca teṣām
          upacaritārthatā/ upakramopasaṃhārādiṣaḍvidhatātparyaliṅgavattayā tattvaṃ bodhayatām
          upacaritārthatvānupapatteḥ/ liṅgaṣaṭkaṃ ca pūrvācāryair darśitam: 
 
 upakramopasaṃhārāv abhyāso ’pūrvatā phalam/ 
 arthavādopapattī ca liṅgaṃ tātparyanirṇaye// iti/ 
 
 [l. 16.164] 
 tatra sad eva saumyedam agra āsīd ity upakramaḥ/ aitadātmyam idaṃ sarvaṃ tat satyaṃ sa
          ātmā tat tvam asi śvetaketo ity upasaṃhāraḥ/ tayor brahmaviṣayatvenaikarūpyam 
 ° aikarūpyam  ]; ° aikyarūpyam  ASS, A. 
  ekaliṅgam/ asakṛt tat tvam asīty uktir abhyāsaḥ/ mānāntarāgamyatvam apūrvatvam/
          ekavijñānena sarvavijñānaṃ phalam/ sṛṣṭisthitipralayapraveśaniyamanāni pañcārthavādāḥ/
          mṛdādidṛṣṭāntā upapattayaḥ/ tasmād etair liṅgair vedāntānāṃ
          nityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvabrahmātmaparatvaṃ niścetavyam/ tad ittham
          aupaniṣadasyātmatattvasyāhamanubhave ’navabhāsamānatvāt
          tasyānubhavasyādhyastātmaviṣayatvaṃ siddham/ 
 [l. 16.172] 
 kaṇabhakṣākṣacaraṇādikakṣīkṛtasyātmano bhānābhāvād ahamanubhavasyādhyastātmaviṣayatvam
          eṣitavyam/ na tāvad ahamanubhavaḥ sarvagatatvam ātmano ’vagamayitum īṣṭe/ aham ihāsmi
          sadane jānāna iti prādeśikatvagrahaṇāt/ na cedaṃ dehasya prādeśikatvaṃ pratibhāsata iti
          veditavyam/ aham ity ullekhāyogāt/ 
 nanu yathā rājñaḥ sarvaprayojanavidhātari bhṛtye mamātmā bhadrasena ity upacāras tadvad
          ātmavacanasyāhaṃśabdasya deha upacāra iti cet 
 maivaṃ vocaḥ/ upacaritātmabhāvasya dehādeḥ svasamānākṛtiśilāputrakādivaj
          jñātṛtvāyogāt/ 
 na ca jñātṛtvam apy upacaritam/ prayoktuḥ svapratipattiprakāśake prayoge
          pratipattṛtvopacārānupapatteḥ/ atha dehadharmaḥ prādeśikatvam ātmany upacaryeta tadā
          dehātmanor bhedena bhavitavyam/ prasiddhabhede māṇavake siṃhaśabdavat sāṃpratikagauṇatve
          tirohitabhedena sārṣapādau rase tailaśabdavan nirūḍhagauṇatve vā gauṇamukhyayor
          bhedādhyavasāyasya niyatatvāt/ 
 atha mama śarīram iti bhedabhānasaṃbhavād gauṇatvaṃ manyethās tad ayuktam/
          ahaṃśabdārthasya dehādibhyo niṣkṛṣyāsādhāraṇadharmavattvena pratibhāsamānatvābhāvāt/
          aparathā lokāyatikamataṃ nodayam āsādayet/ mama śarīram ity uktis tu rāhoḥ śira itivad
          aupacārikī/ mama śarīram iti bruvāṇenāpi kas tvam iti pṛṣṭena vakṣasthalanyastahastena
          śṛṅgagrāhikayāyam aham iti prativacanasya dīyamānatvena dehātmapratyayasya
          sakalānubhavasiddhatvāt/ tad uktam : 
 [l. 16.191] 
 
 dehātmapratyayo yadvat pramāṇatvena kalpitaḥ/ 
 laukikaṃ tadvad evedaṃ pramāṇaṃ tv ātmaniścayāt// iti// 
 
 tathā ca vyāpakasya bhedabhānasya nivṛtter vyāpyasya gauṇatvasya nivṛttir iti
          niravadyam/ 
 [l. 16.195] 
 nanv abhijñayā bhedasiddhir mā saṃbhūn nāma/ pratyabhijñayā tu so ’ham ity evaṃrūpayā
          tatsiddhiḥ saṃbhaviṣyatīti cen 
 na/ vikalpāsahatvāt/ kim iyaṃ pratyabhijñā pāmarāṇāṃ syāt parīkṣakāṇāṃ vā/ nādyaḥ/
          dehavyatiriktātmaikyam avagāhamānāyāḥ pratyabhijñāyā anudayāt/ pratyuta śyāmasya
          lauhityavat kāraṇaviśeṣād alpasyāpi mahāparimāṇatvam aviruddham anubhavatāṃ taddeha eva
          tasyāḥ saṃbhavāc ca/ na dvitīyaḥ/ vyavahārasamaye pāmarasāmyānatirekāt/ aparokṣabhramasya
          parokṣajñānavināśyatvānupapatteś ca/ yad uktaṃ bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa paśvādibhiś
          cāviśeṣāt iti/ bhāmatīkārair apy uktaṃ śāstracintakāḥ khalv evaṃ vicārayanti na
          pratipattāra iti/ tathā cātmagocarasyādhyāsātmarūpatvaṃ sustham/ 
 [l. 16.206] 
 na cārhatamatānusāreṇāhaṃpratyayaprāmāṇyāyātmano dehaparimāṇatvam aṅgīkaraṇīyam iti
          sāṃpratam/ madhyamaparimāṇasya sāvayavatvena dehādivad anityatve
          kṛtahānākṛtābhyāgamaprasaṅgāt/ athaitaddoṣaparijihīrṣayāvayavasamudāya ātmety
          abhyupagamyeta tadā vaktavyam/ kiṃ pratyekam avayavānāṃ caitanyaṃ saṃghātasya vā/ nādyaḥ/
          bahūnāṃ cetanānām ahamahamikayā pradhānabhāvam anubhavatām aikamatyābhāvena samasamayaṃ
          viruddhadikkriyatayā śarīrasyāpi viśaraṇaniṣkriyatvayor anyatarāpātāt/ dvitīye ’pi
          saṃghātāpattiḥ kiṃ śarīropādhikī svābhāvikī yādṛcchikī vā/ nādyaḥ/ ekasminn avayave chinne
          cidātmano ’py avayavaś chinna ity acetanatvāpātāt/ na dvitīyaḥ/ anekeṣām avayavānām
          anyonyasāhityaniyamādarśanāt/ na tṛtīyaḥ/ saṃśleṣavad viśleṣasyāpi yādṛcchikatvena sukhena
          vasatām akasmād acetanatvaprasaṅgāt/ 
 [l. 16.218] 
 na cāṇuparimāṇatvam ātmanaḥ śaṅkanīyam/ sthūlo ’haṃ dīrgho ’ham iti
          pratyayānupapatteḥ/ 
 [l. 16.220] 
 na ca vijñānātmabhāṣiṇāṃ naiṣa doṣaḥ/ viśuddhasāvayavatvābhāvād iti gaṇanīyam/ yaḥ
          suṣuptaḥ so ’haṃ jāgarmīti sthiragocarasyāhamullekhasya kṣaṇabhaṅgivijñānagocaratve
          atasmiṃstadbuddhirūpamithyādhyāsasya tadavasthānāt/ tad anena kṛśo ’haṃ kṛṣṇo ’ham
          ityādīnāṃ prakhyātānānāṃ buddhyā sarūpatākhyānenaupacārikatvaṃ pratyākhyātam/
          tadvyāpakabhedabhānāsaṃbhavasya prāg eva prapañcitatvāt/ tathā ca prayogaḥ: 
 vimataṃ śāstraṃ viṣayaprayojanasahitam 
 āvidyakabandhanivartakatvāt 
 suptothitabodhavat/ 
 yathā svapnāvasthāyāṃ māyāparikalpitayoṣādikṛtabandhanivartakasya suptotthitabodhasya
          mandiramadhye sukhena śayyāyām avatiṣṭhamāno deho viṣayaḥ/ tasya suptabodhenāniścayāt/
          svapnamāyāvijṛmbhitānarthanivṛttiḥ prayojanam/ evaṃ
          mananādijanyaparokṣajñānadvāreṇādhyāsikakartṛtva-bhoktṛtvādyanarthaniṣedhakasya śāstrasya
          saccidānandaikarasaṃ pratyagātmabhūtaṃ brahma viṣayaḥ/ tasyāhamanubhavenāniścayāt/
          adhyāsanivṛttiḥ prayojanam/ tathā cāphalatvād iti hetur asiddha iti siddham/ tad
          uktam : 
 [l. 16.234] 
 
 śrutigamyātmatattvaṃ tu nāhaṃbuddhyāvagamyate/ 
 api khe kāmato mohā nātmany astaviparyaye// iti/ 
 
 ito ’yam asaṃdigdhatvād iti hetur apy asiddha iti siddham/ 
 [l. 16.237] 
 yady api sarvaḥ prāṇī pratyagātmāstitvaṃ pratyety aham asmīti/ na hi kaścid api nāham
          asmīti vipratipadyate/ pratyagātmaiva brahma tat tvam asi iti sāmānādhikaraṇyāt/ tasmād
          ātmatattvam asaṃdigdhaṃ siddham/ tathāpi dharmaṃ prati vipratipannā bahuvidhā iti nyāyena
          viśeṣapratipattir upapadyata eva/ tathā hi/ caitanyaviśiṣṭaṃ deham ātmeti lokāyatā
          manyante/ indriyāṇy ātmety anye/ antaḥkaraṇam ātmety apare/ kṣaṇabhaṅguraṃ saṃtanyamānaṃ
          vijñānam ātmeti bauddhā budhyante/ dehaparimāṇa ātmeti jainā jināḥ pratijānate/
          kartṛtvādiviśiṣṭaḥ parameśvarād bhinno jīvātmeti naiyāyikādayo varṇayanti/
          dravyabodhasvabhāvam ātmety ācāryāḥ paricakṣate/ bhoktaiva kevalaṃ na karteti sāṃkhyāḥ
          saṃgirante/ cidrūpaḥ kartṛtvādirahitaḥ parasmād abhinnaḥ pratyagātmety aupaniṣadā
          bhāṣante/ evaṃ prasiddhe dharmiṇi viśeṣato vipratipattau tadviśeṣasaṃśayo yujyate/ tathā
          ca saṃdehasaṃbhavāj jijñāsyatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ siddham/ tad itthaṃ brahmaṇo
          vicāryatvasaṃbhavena tadvicārātmakaṃ brahmamīmāṃsāśāstram āraṃbhaṇīyam iti yuktam/ janmādy
          asya yataḥ ityādisarvasya śāstrasyaitadvicārāpekṣatvāc chāstraprathamādhyāyasaṃgatam idam
          adhikaraṇam/ 
 [l. 16.254] 
 nanv itthaṃbhūte brahmaṇi kiṃ pramāṇaṃ pratyakṣam anumānam āgamo vā/ na kadācit tatra
          pratyakṣaṃ śramate/ atīndriyatvāt/ nāpy anumānam/ vyāptasya liṅgasyābhāvāt/ nāpy āgamaḥ/
          yato vāco nivartante iti śrutyaivāgamagamyatvaniṣedhāt/ upamānādikam aśakyaśaṅkam/
          niyataviṣayatvāt/ tasmād brahmaṇi pramāṇaṃ na saṃbhavatīti cet 
 maivaṃ vocaḥ/ pratyakṣādyasaṃbhave ’py āgamasya sattvāt/ 
 yato vāco nivartante iti vāggocaratvaniṣedhāt katham etad iti cet 
 śrutir eva niṣedhati vedāntavedyatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutir eva vidhatte/ na hi
          vedapratipādite ’rthe ’nupapanne vaidikānāṃ buddhiḥ khidyate/ api tu tadupapādanamārgam
          eva vicārayati/ tasmād ubhayam api pratipādanīyam/ viṣayatvaniṣedhakāni vākyāni/
          vākyajanyavṛttivyaktasphuraṇalakṣaṇaphalāsaṃbhavavivakṣayā pravṛttāni/ viṣayatvabodhakāni
          tu vṛttijanyāvaraṇabhaṅgalakṣaṇaphalasaṃbhavavivakṣayā/ tad uktaṃ bhagavadbhiḥ : 
 
 anādheyaphalatvena śruter brahma na gocaram/ 
 prameyaṃ pramitau tu syād ātmākārasamarpaṇāt// iti/ 
 na prakāśyaṃ pramāṇena prakāśo brahmaṇaḥ svayam/ 
 tajjanyāvṛtibhaṅgatvāt prameyam iti gīyate// iti ca/ 
 
 [l. 16.271] 
 nanu syād eṣa manoratho yadi siddhe ’rthe vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ sidhyet/
          saṃgatigrahaṇāyattatvāt/ vṛddhavyavahārasya ca loke kāryaikaniyatatvāt/ na hy asti
          saṃbhavaḥ śabdānāṃ kārye ’rthe saṃgatigrahe 
 saṃgatigrahe  ];  saṃgatigrahaḥ  ASS, A. 
  siddhārthābhidhāyakatvaṃ tatra vā prāmāṇyam iti/ na hi turaṅgatve gṛhītasaṃgatikaṃ
          turaṅgapadaṃ gotvam ācaṣṭe tatra vā prāmāṇyaṃ bhajate/ tasmāt kāryagṛhītasaṃgatikānāṃ
          śabdānāṃ kārya eva prāmāṇyam/ 
 nanu mukhavikāsādiliṅgād dharṣahetuṃ prasiddhārtham anumāya yatra śabdasya saṃgatigraho
          yathā putras te jāta ityādiṣu tatrāvaśyaṃ kāryam antareṇaiva śabdasya siddhe ’rthe
          prāmāṇyam āśrīyata iti cen 
 na/ putrajanmavad eva priyāsukhaprasavāder anekasya harṣahetor upasthīyamānatvena
          pariśeṣāvadhāraṇānupapatteḥ/ putras te jāta ityādiṣu siddhārthapareṣu prayogeṣu dvāraṃ
          dvāram ityādivat kāryādhyāhāreṇa prayogopapatteś ca/ śāstratvaprasiddhyā ca na vedāntānāṃ
          siddhārthatvaparatvam/ pravṛttinivṛttiparāṇām eva vākyānāṃ śāstratvaprasiddheḥ/ tad uktaṃ
          bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ : 
 [l. 16.286] 
 
 pravṛttir vā nivṛttir vā nityena kṛtakena vā/ 
 puṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tac chāstram abhidhīyate// iti/ 
 
 na caiteṣāṃ svarūpaparatve prayojanam asti/ śrutavedāntārthasyāpi puṃsaḥ
          sāṃsārikadharmāṇām anivṛtteḥ/ tasmād vedāntānām apy ātmā jñātavya iti samāmnātena
          vidhinaikavākyatām āśritya kāryaparataivāśrayaṇīyeti siddham/ tataś ca kevalasiddharūpe
          brahmaṇi vedāntānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ na sidhyatīti cet/ 
 [l. 16.293] 
 atra pratividhīyate: na tāvad siddhe vyutpattyasiddhiḥ/ prāg unnītayā nītyā putras te
          jāta iti vākyāt siddhaparād api vyutpattisiddheḥ/ na ca pariśeṣāvadhāraṇānupapattiḥ/
          priyāsukhaprasavāder api saṃbhavād iti bhaṇitavyam/ putrapadāṅkitapaṭapradarśanavat
          priyāsukhaprasavādisūcakābhāvāt/ putrajanmaiva tatsūcakam iti cen na 
 cen na  ];  cet 
              ASS, A. 
 
 prathamapratītaputrajanmaparityāge kāraṇābhāvāt/ putrajananasyaivādhikānandahetutvāc
          ca/ 
 
 putrotpattivipattibhyāṃ nāparaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ/ 
 
 iti vidyamānatvāt/ tathā cācakathac citsukhācāryaḥ: 
 
 dṛṣṭacaitrasutotpattes tatpadāṅkitavāsasā/ 
 vārtāhāreṇa yātasya pariśeṣaviniściteḥ// 
 
 [l. 16.304] 
 yad uktaṃ siddhārthapareṣu kāryādhyāhāra iti tad ayuktam/ mukhyārthaviṣayatayā siddhe ’pi
          prayogasiddhāv adhyāhārānupapatteḥ/ yad uktaṃ śāstratvaprasiddhyā ca na svarūpaparatvam
          iti tad apy ayuktam/ hitaśāsanād api śāstratvopapatteḥ/ na ca prayojanābhāvaḥ/
          śrutamatavedāntajanyādvitīyātmavijñānābhyāsena vidyodaye
          saṃsāranidānāvidyānivṛttyupalakṣitabrahmātmatālakṣaṇaparamapuruṣārtha-siddheḥ/ na cātra
          vidhiḥ saṃbhavati/ vikalpāsahatvāt/ tathā hi : kiṃ śābdajñānaṃ vidheyaṃ kiṃ vā
          bhāvanātmakam āhosvit sākṣātkārarūpam/ nādyaḥ/
          viditapadārthasaṃgatikasyādhītaśabdanyāyatattvasyāntareṇāpi vidhiṃ śabdād evopapatteḥ/
          nāpi dvitīyaḥ/ bhāvanāyā jñānaprakarṣahetubhāvasyānvayavyatirekasiddhatayā
          prāptatvenāvidheyatvāt/ aprāptaprāpakasyaiva vidhitvāṅgīkārāt/ tṛtīye sākṣātkāraḥ kiṃ
          brahmasvarūpaḥ kiṃ vāntaḥkaraṇapariṇāmabhedaḥ/ nādyaḥ/ tasya nityatvenāvidheyatvāt/ nāpi
          dvitīyaḥ/ ānandasākṣātkārarūpatayā phalatvenāvidheyatvāt/ tasmāj jñātavya ityādīnām
          avidhāyakatvād arhe kṛtyatṛcaś ca iti kṛtyapratyayānām arhārthe vidhānād arhārthataiva
          vyākhyeyā/ tathā ca sarveṣāṃ vedāntavākyānām upakramopasaṃhārādiṣaḍvidhatātparyopetatvān
          nityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvabrahmātmaparatvam āstheyam/ 
 [l. 16.322] 
 niṣpradeśe paramāṇau pradeśavṛttitvenābhimatasya saṃyogasya durupapādanatayā
          tannibandhanasya dvyaṇukasyāsiddhau dvyaṇukādikrameṇārambhavādāsaṃbhavād acetanāyāḥ
          prakṛter mahadādirūpeṇa pariṇāmavādāsaṃbhavāc ca khyātibādhānyathānupapattyānirvacanīyaḥ
          prapañcaś cidvivarta iti siddham/ svarūpāparityāgena rūpāntarāpattir vivarta iti
          satyamithyākhyāvabhāsa iti/ avabhāso ’dhyāsa iti paryāyaḥ/ sa cādhyāso dvividhaḥ :
          arthādhyāso jñānādhyāsaś ceti/ tad uktam : 
 
 pramāṇadoṣasaṃskārajanmānyasya parātmatā/ 
 taddhīś cādhyāsa iti hi dvayam iṣṭaṃ manīṣibhiḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 16.331] 
 punar api dvividho ’dhyāsaḥ/ nirupādhikasopādhikabhedāt/ tad apy uktam : 
 
 doṣeṇa karmaṇā vāpi kṣobhitājñānasaṃbhavaḥ/ 
 tattvavidyāvirodhī ca bhramo ’yaṃ nirupādhikaḥ// 
 upādhisaṃnidhiprāptakṣobhāvidyāvijṛmbhitam/ 
 upādhyapagamāpohyam āhuḥ sopādhikaṃ bhramam// iti/ 
 
 tatra svarūpeṇa kalpitāhamādyadhyāso nirupādhikaḥ/ tad apy uktam : 
 
 nīlimeva viyaty eṣā bhrāntyā brahmaṇi saṃsṛtiḥ/ 
 ghaṭavyomeva bhoktāyaṃ bhrānto bhedena na svataḥ// iti/ 
 
 ata eva bhāṣyakāraḥ śuktikā rajatavad avabhāsata ekaś candraḥ sadvitīyavad iti
          nidarśanadvayam udājahāra/ śiṣṭaṃ śāstra eva spaṣṭam iti vistarabhiyoparamyate/ evaṃ ca
          dṛgdṛśyau dvāv eva padārthāv iti vedāntināṃ siddhānta iti sarvam avadātam/ 
 [l. 16.344] 
 atra prabhākaraḥ : śuktikā rajatavad avabhāsata iti dṛṣṭānto neṣṭaḥ/ rajatapratyayasya
          śuktikālambanatvānupapatteḥ/ tathā hi : idaṃ rajatam iti pratītau śukter ālambanatvaṃ
          purodeśasattāmātreṇāvalambyate kāraṇatvena bhāsamānatvena vā/ nādyaḥ/ purovartināṃ
          loṣṭādīnām apy ālambanatvaprasaṅgāt/ atha kaladhautabodhakaraṇasaṃskārodbodhakāraṇatvena
          taddvārā rajatajñānakāraṇatvād ālambanatvaṃ manyase/ tad api na saṃgacchate/ cakṣurādīnām
          api kāraṇatvena viṣayatvāpātāt/ atha bhāsamānatayā viṣayatvam iṣyate tad apy aśliṣṭam/
          rajatanirbhāsasya śuktikālambanatvānupapatteḥ/ yasmin vijñāne yad avabhāsate tat
          tadālambanam/ atra ca kaladhautānubhavaḥ śuktikālambanatvakalpanāyāṃ virudhyate/ tathā
          cācakathan nyāyavīthyāṃ śālikanāthaḥ : 
 
 atra brūmo ya evārtho yasyāṃ saṃvidi bhāsate/ 
 vedyaḥ sa eva nānyad dhi vedyāvedyatvalakṣaṇam// 
 idaṃ rajatam ity atra rajataṃ tv avabhāsate/ 
 tad eva tena vedyaṃ syān na tu śuktir avedanāt// 
 tenānyasyānyathā bhāsaḥ pratītyaiva parāhataḥ/ 
 anyasmin bhāsamāne hi na paraṃ bhāsate yataḥ// iti/ 
 
 [l. 16.362] 
 kiṃ ca mithyājānānotpattau sāmagrī na samasti/ kiṃ kevalānīndriyādīni kāraṇāni
          doṣadūṣitāni vā/ nādyaḥ/ teṣāṃ samīcīnajñānajananasāmarthyopalambhāt/ anyathā samīcīnaṃ
          rajatajñānaṃ kadācid udayam āsādayet/ na dvitīyaḥ/ doṣāṇām
          autsargikakāryaprasavaśaktipratibandhamātraprabhāvatvāt/ na hi duṣṭaṃ kuṭajabījaṃ
          vaṭāṅkuraṃ janayitum īṣṭe/ na vā tailakaluṣitaṃ śālibījam aśālyaṅkurajananāyālam/ kiṃ tu
          svakāryaṃ na karoti/ 
 nanu dāvadahanadagdhasya vetrabījasya kadalīkāṇḍajanakatvaṃ dṛṣṭam iti cet 
 tan na sthāne/ dagdhasyāvetrabījatvena doṣāṇāṃ viparītakāryakāritvaṃ praty anudāharaṇāt/
          na ca bhasmakadoṣadūṣitasya kaukṣeyasyāśuśukṣaṇer bahvannapacanasāmarthyaṃ dṛṣṭam ity
          eṣṭavyam/ aśitapītādyāhārapariṇatau jāṭharasya jātavedasaḥ śaktatvāt/ tad uktam : 
 
 ayathārthasya bodhasya notpattāv asti kāraṇam/ 
 doṣāś cen na hi doṣāṇāṃ kāryaśaktivighātatā// 
 bhasmakādiṣu kāryasya vighātād eva doṣatā/ 
 agner hi rasaniṣpattiḥ kāryaṃ jaṭharavartinaḥ// 
 
 [l. 16.379] 
 api cāsaty apy arthe jñānaprādurbhāvābhyupagame samīcīnasthale ’pi jñānānāṃ
          svagocaravyabhicāraśaṅkāṅkurasaṃbhavena niraṅkuśo vyavahāro lupyate/ tad āha: 
 
 yadi cārthaṃ parityajya kācid buddhiḥ prakāśate/ 
 vyābhicāravati svārthe kathaṃ viśvāsakāraṇam// 
 
 [l. 16.385] 
 nanu rajatagocaraikaviśiṣṭajñānānaṅgīkāre viśiṣṭavyavahāro na sidhyet/ atas tatsiddhaye
          ’pi viparyayo ’ṅgīkārya iti cen 
 na/ idaṃ rajatam iti grahaṇasmaraṇābhidhasya bodhadvayasya vyavahārakāraṇatvāṅgīkārāt/
          yady evaṃ idaṃ śuktikāśakalaṃ tad rajatam ity ato ’pi viśiṣṭavyavahāraḥ syād iti/ tan na/
          tatredam iti purovartidravyamātragrahaṇasya
          doṣadūṣitacakṣurjanyatvenānākalitaśuktitvādiviśeṣitasya sāmānyamātragrahaṇarūpatvād
          rajatam iti jñānasyāsaṃnihitaviṣayasya saṃprayogaliṅgādyaprasūtatayā
          sadṛśāvabodhitasaṃskāramātraprabhavatvena pariśeṣaprāptasmṛtibhāvasya doṣahetukatayā
          gṛhītatattāṃśapramoṣād grahaṇamātratvopapatteḥ/ tad apy uktam : 
 
 nanv atra rajatābhāsaḥ katham eṣa ghaṭiṣyate/ 
 ucyate śuktiśakalaṃ gṛhītaṃ bhedavarjitam// 
 śuktikāyā viśeṣā ye rajatād bhedahetavaḥ/ 
 te na jñātā abhibhavāj jñātā sāmānyarūpatā// 
 anantaraṃ ca rajatasmṛtir jātā tayāpi ca/ 
 manodoṣāt tad ity aṃśaparāmarśavivarjitam// 
 rajataṃ viṣayīkṛtya naiva śukter vivecitam/ 
 smṛtyāto rajatābhāsa upapanno bhaviṣyati// 
 na hy asaṃnihitaṃ tāvat pratyakṣaṃ rajataṃ bhavet/

 pariśeṣāt smṛtir iti niścayo jāyate punaḥ/

 ° ayukto ° ]; ° anukto ° ASS, A. 
 pālambho ’yam iti cet 
 tad apy ayuktam/ vikalpāsahatvāt/ tathā hi: samīcīnarajatāvabhāsasārūpyaṃ bhāsamānaṃ
          pravartakaṃ sattāmātreṇa vā/ ādye vikalpe bhedāgrahāparaparyāyasya sārūpyasya
          samīcīnasaṃnibhe ime jñāne iti viśeṣākāreṇa gṛhyamāṇasya pravṛttikāraṇatvaṃ kiṃ vānayor
          eva svarūpato viṣayataś ca mitho bhedāgraho vidyata iti sāmānyākāreṇa gṛhyamāṇasya
          sārūpyasya/ nādyaḥ/ samīcīnajñānavat tatsaṃnibhajñānasya
          taducitavyavahārapravartakatvānupapatteḥ/ na khalu gosaṃnibho gavaya ity avabhāso
          gavārthinaṃ gavaye pravartayati/ na dvitīyaḥ/ vyāhatatvāt/ na khalv anākalitabhedasyānayor
          iti anayor iti grahe bhedāgraha iti ca pratipattir bhavati/ ataḥ pariśeṣāt sattāmātreṇa
          bhedāgraharūpasya sārūpyasya vyavahārakāraṇatvam aṅgīkartavyam/ evam evāstv iti cet,
          tarhīdam iha saṃpradhāryam: kim ayaṃ bhedāgrahaḥ samāropotpādanakrameṇa vyavahārakāraṇam
          astūtānutpāditāropa eva svayam iti/ na ca dvitīyaḥ pakṣa eva śreyān/ tāvataiva
          vyavahārotpattāv āropasya gauravadoṣaduṣṭatvād iti mantavyam/ viśiṣṭavyavahārasya
          viśiṣṭajñānapūrvakatvaniyamenājñānapūrvakatvānupapatteḥ/ 
 [l. 16.514] 
 nanv ayaṃ vyavahāro nājñānapūrvaka ity anākalitaparābhisaṃdhiḥ svasiddhāntasiddhārthād
          yadi kaścic chaṅketa sa prativaktavyaḥ/ śuktikāviṣayasya grahaṇasyāsamīhitaviṣayatvena
          rajatārthipravṛttihetutvāsaṃbhavād anvayavyatirekābhyāṃ rajatajñānasya samīhitaviṣayatvena
          pravṛttihetutvasaṃbhavāc cedamarthābhisaṃbhinnagrahaviviktasyāpi rajatasmaraṇasya
          kāraṇatvaṃ vaktavyam/ tac ca vaktuṃ na śakyate/ jānāti icchati tataḥ pravartata iti
          nyāyena jñānecchāpravṛttīnāṃ samānaviṣayatvena bhāvyam/ tathā

          anyad vyavaharatīti vyāhanyeta/ tathā ca yadīdaṃkārāspadaṃ rajatāvabhāsagocaratāṃ nācaret
          kathaṃ rajatārthī tad icchet/ yady arajatatvāgrahaṇād iti brūyāt/ rajatatvāgrahāt kasmād
          ayaṃ nopekṣeteti/ yugapat tadbhavabhedāgrahābhedāgrahanibandhanābhyāṃ purataḥ pṛṣṭhataś
          cākṛṣyamāṇaḥ puruṣo dolāyamānatayā rūpyāropam antareṇopādānapakṣa eva na vyavasthāpyata
          ity anicchatāpy acchamatinā samāropaḥ samāśrayaṇīyaḥ/ yathāha: bhedāgrahād idaṃkārāspade
          rajatatvam āropya tajjātīyasyopakārahetubhāvam anusmṛtya tajjātīyatvenāsyāpi tad anumāya
          tadarthī pravartata iti prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ praśasyaḥ/

 tad api vaktum aśakyam/ śakyasya durnirūpyatvāt/

 nanu vijñānavādinayānusāreṇa pratīyamānaṃ rajataṃ jñānātmakam/ tatra ca yuktir

          āsthīyata ity ubhayavādisaṃmato ’rthaḥ/ tatra ca nedaṃ rajatam iti niṣiddhedaṃbhāvaṃ
          rajatam arthād āntarajñānarūpam avatiṣṭhate/ na cedaṃtayā niṣedhe saty anidaṃtayā ca bahir

          sākṣipratyakṣe bhāvarūpājñāne vartata iti savyabhicāraḥ/ 
 [l. 16.615] 
 nanv anyathākhyātivādimatānusāreṇa rajatasya deśāntarasattvena bhāvyam/ anyathā tasya
          pratiṣedhapratiyogitvānupapatteḥ/ na hi kaścit prekṣāvāñ śaśaviṣāṇaṃ pratiṣeddhuṃ
          prabhavati/ tad uktam : 
 
 vyāvartyābhāvavattaiva bhāvikī hi viśeṣyatā/ 
 abhāvavirahātmatvaṃ vastunaḥ pratiyogitā// iti/ 
 
 tathā ca tasya deśāntarasattvam āśrayaṇīyam iti cet 
 tad api na pramāṇapaddhatim adhyāste/ asataḥ saṃsargasyeva kaladhautasya
          niṣedhapratiyogitvopapatteḥ/ 
 [l. 16.624] 
 nanv idaṃ rajatam iti jñānam ekam anekaṃ vā/ na tāvad ādyaḥ/ apasiddhāntāpatter
          asaṃbhavāc ca/ tathā hi/ śuktīdamaṃśendriyasaṃprayogād idamākārāntaḥkaraṇa 
 ° rāntaḥkaraṇa ° ]; ° rāntaḥ ° A. 
 pariṇāmarūpam ekaṃ jñānaṃ jāyate/ na ca tatra kaladhautaṃ viṣayabhāvam ākalpayitum
          utsahate/ asaṃprayuktatvāt tasya/ viṣayatvāṅgīkāre sarvajñatvāpatteḥ/ na ca
          cakṣuranvayavyatirekānuvidhāyitayā tajjñānasya tajjanyatvaṃ vācyam/ idamaṃśajñānotpattau
          tadupakṣayopapatteḥ/ na cāpi saṃskārād rajatajñānasya janma/ smṛtitvāpatteḥ/
          athendriyadoṣasya tatkaraṇatvam/ tad apy ayuktam/ svātantryeṇa tasya
          jñānahetutvānupapatteḥ/ na hi grahaṇasmaraṇābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ samasti/ tasmād
          idamaṃśarajatatādātmyaviṣayam ekaṃ vijñānaṃ na ghaṭate/ nāpy anekam akhyātimatāpatter iti
          cet — 
 [l. 16.635] 
 ucyate/ prathamaṃ doṣakaluṣitena cakṣuṣedaṃtāmātraviṣayāntaḥkaraṇavṛttir utpadyate/
          anantaraṃ tayā vṛttyā caitanyāvaraṇābhibhave sati tac caitanyam abhivyajyate/ paścād

          sākṣicaitanyenāvyavadhānena bhāsyete/ tathā ca savṛttikāyā avidyāyāḥ
          sākṣibhāsyatvābhyupagame vṛttyantaravedyatvābhāvān nānavasthā/ yady apy antaḥkaraṇavṛttir
          avidyāvṛttiś ceti dve ime jñāne tathāpi viṣayādhīnaṃ phalam/ jñāto ghaṭa iti

 [l. 16.648] 
 
 śuktīdamaṃśacaitanyasthitāvidyā vijṛmbhate/ 
 rāgādidoṣasaṃskārasacivā rajatātmanā//

 tad ayuktam/ anirvacanīyatvatattvābhāsapratibandhakatvādilakṣaṇajātasya māyāvidyayoḥ
          samānatvāt/ kiṃ cāśrayaśabdena draṣṭocyate kartā vā/ nādyaḥ/

 [l. 16.691] 
 
 māyā vikṣipad ajñānam īśecchāvaśavarti vā/

 [l. 16.693] 
 nanv avidyāsadbhāve kiṃ pramāṇam/ aham ajño mām anyaṃ ca na jānāmīti  pratyakṣa pratibhāsa eva/ nanu jñānābhāvaviṣayo ’yaṃ
          nābhipretam arthaṃ gamayatīti cet — na tāvad anupalabdhivādinaś codyam etat/
          parokṣapratibhāsahetutvāt tasyāḥ/ ayam api parokṣapratibhāsa eveti cet — na tāval
          liṅgaśabdānupapadyamānārthajanyaḥ/ jñātakaraṇatvāt teṣām/ na caitat sāmagrīkāle jñānam
          asti/ anubhūyate vā/ anupalabdhyā janyata iti cet — na tāvad iyam ajñātā karaṇam/

          jñānābhāvagrahaṇe karaṇaṃ na bhavaty eveti vakṣyate/ 
 [l. 16.705] 
 pratyakṣābhāvavāde tu pratyakṣeṇa tāvad dharmipratiyogijñānayoḥ sator ātmani
          jñānamātrābhāvagrahaṇaṃ na brūyāt/ ghaṭavati bhūtale ghaṭābhāvasyeva jñānamātrābhāvasya
          grahītum aśakyatvāt/ tayor asatos tu sutarām/ kāraṇābhāvāt/ ato ’pi yogyānupalabdhyā vā
          phalaliṅgādyabhāvena vātmani jñānamātrābhāvagrahaṇaṃ durlabham iti paramate ’py ayaṃ
          nyāyaḥ samānaḥ/ tad evam ātmani pratyakṣeṇa vānyena vā jñānamātrābhāvasya grahaṇam aśakyam
          iti sthitam/ 
 [l. 16.712] 
 nanu jñānaviśeṣābhāvaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyatām/ na tāvat smaraṇābhāvaḥ/ abhāvagrahaṇe
          pratiyogismaraṇasya kāraṇatvāt/ nāpy anubhavābhāvaḥ/ tasyāvarjanīyatvāt/ nanv ātmani
          ghaṭānubhavābhāvaḥ pratyakṣaviṣayas tarhy aham ajña iti jñānasāmānyavacano jānātir

          vartate/ saṃbandhas tāvad anubhavatvajñānatvayor ekavyaktisamāveśo vyāpyavyāpakabhāvo vā
          vidyata eva/ anupapattiṃ tu na paśyāmaḥ/ 
 nanv anubhavābhāve pratyakṣasya prameyalābhas tenaiva tasyārthavattā sidhyati/ 
 satyam/ prayojanam etan nānupapattiḥ/ anyonyāśrayāt/ 
 nanv aham ajña ity atra nañ ātmani jñānamātrābhāvaṃ na brūte/ jñānavati tasmiṃs
          tadabhāvāt/ nāpy anubhavābhāvam/ jñānoktes tadanabhidhāyakatvāt/ nairarthakyaṃ ca na
          yuktam ity anayaivānupapattyā lakṣaṇeti cet — 
 uktalakṣaṇaivāvidyā tadartho ’stu/ 
 saṃdeha iti cen na/ 
 asamatvāt koṭidvayasya/ anyatra hi pratiyoginivṛttir nañarthaḥ/ atra tu
          pratiyogivyāpyanivṛttir iti/ jānātisamabhivyāhṛtasya nañaḥ kvacid
          uktalakṣaṇāvidyāviṣayatvasiddhim antareṇa na saṃdeha ity avaśyaṃbhāvena saiva
          jānātisamabhivyāhṛtasya nañaḥ sarvatra tadviṣayatvam avagamayati vilumpati
          jñānābhāvakoṭyantaram iti kva saṃdehāvakāśaḥ/ tad evaṃ lakṣaṇāhetvabhāve ’nubhavābhāvo ’py
          ātmani na pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti pariśeṣād uktalakṣaṇāvidyaivājña iti pratibhāsasya
          viṣaya iti sthitam/ 
 [l. 16.732] 
 astu vā jñānābhāvapratibhāsaḥ/ ayam abhāvaś ca pratiyogī yatra niṣidhyate na tatas
          tattvāntaram anyadadhikaraṇabhāvāt/ mā bhūd anyabhāvatvam anyābhāvatvaṃ tu syāt/ nanu tad
          api viruddham/ satyaṃ sati bhede/ sa ca pramāṇāt/ tac ca sati pratiyogyabhāvādhikaraṇatas
          tattvāntare/ nanu ghaṭavati bhūtale ghaṭābhāvamitivyavahṛtī syātām iti cet — mā bhūtām ete
          pratiyoginā sahānubhūyamāne ’dhikaraṇe/ pratiyogismaraṇe saty anubhūyamāne ’dhikaraṇe tu
          syātām/ evam apy upapattau na tattvāntaraviṣayatvaṃ kalpyam/ kānupapattir iti ced
          bādhakābhāvas tāvad ukta eva/ bādhakaṃ tu kalpanāgauravam eva/ tathā hi tattvāntaratvaṃ
          tāvad ekaṃ kalpyam/ tasyāparokṣatvāyendriyasaṃnikarṣaḥ kalpyaḥ/ sa ca saṃyogādir na
          bhavatīti saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇatvādiḥ kalpya ity ato varam uktalakṣaṇasyādhikaraṇasya
          vyavahāraviṣaye ’ṅgīkāraḥ/ sati caivaṃ jñānābhāvenāpi pratiyogismṛtau satyām anubhūyamānam
          adhikaraṇaṃ jñātaiva/ sa ca na kevalam antaḥkaraṇam/ jaḍatvāt/ nāpi kevala ātmaiva/

          āyātam avidyāyām evāham ajña iti pratibhāsaḥ pramāṇam iti/ 
 [l. 16.749] 
 anumānaṃ ca — vivādapadaṃ pramāṇajñānaṃ
          svaprāgabhāvavyatirikta-svaviṣayāvaraṇasvanivartyasvadeśagatavastvantarapūrvakam
          aprakāśitārthaprakāśakatvāt/ andhakāre prathamotpannapradīpaprabhāvad iti/ vastupūrvakam
          ity ukta ātmavastupūrvakatvenārthāntaratā/ tadarthaṃ vastvantareti/ tathāpi viṣayabhūte
          vastvantare ’rthāntaratā/ tadarthaṃ svadeśagateti/ adṛṣṭādikaṃ pratyādeṣṭuṃ svanivartyeti/
          uttarajñānanivartyaṃ prathamajñānaṃ nivartayituṃ svaviṣayāvaraṇeti/ prāgabhāvaṃ
          pratikṣeptuṃ svaprāgabhāvavyatirikteti/ svaprāgabhāvavyatiriktapūrvakam ity ukte
          viṣayeṇārthāntaratā/ tadarthaṃ viṣayāvaraṇeti/ tādṛśam andhakāraṃ vyāseddhuṃ
          svanivartyeti/ viṣayagatām ajñātatāṃ nirākartuṃ svadeśagateti/ mithyājñānam apohituṃ
          vastvantareti/ dhārāvāhikavijñāne vyabhicāraṃ vyāseddhum aprakāśiteti/
          madhyavartipradīpaprabhāyāṃ sādhyasādhanavaidhuryapratirodhāya prathamotpannaviśeṣaṇam/
          saurālokavyāptadeśasthapradīpaprabhāpratikṣepāyāndhakāreti/ 
 na ca jñānasādhake pramāṇe vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkanīyaḥ/ vipratipannaṃ praty
          asattvanivṛttimātrasya pramāṇakṛtyatvāt/ tad uktaṃ devatādhikaraṇe kalpatarukārair
          anumānādibhir asattvanivṛttiḥ kriyata iti/ nanu sādhanavikalo dṛṣṭānta iti cen na/

          śaṅkanīyaḥ/ tamovirodhyākāro hi prakāśaśabdavācyaḥ/ tenākāreṇaikyam ubhayatrāstīti/
          narendragiriśrīcaraṇais tv ittham uktam — aprakāśitaprakāśavyavahārahetutvaṃ hetvarthaḥ/
          tasya cobhayatrānugatatvān nāsiddhyādir iti/

 śruteś ca/ bhūyaś cānte viśvamāyānivṛttiḥ ityādikā śrutiḥ/

 [l. 16.781] 
 kecana śāktāḥ — śaktiṃ māyāśabdārthabhūtāṃ jagatkāraṇatvenāṅgīkṛtāṃ satyām abhyupetya
          mātuliṅgagadākheṭavidhāriṇī mahālakṣmīs tasyāḥ prathamāvatāra iti varṇayanti/ sā ca

          āsa/ svayaṃ mithunaṃ janayitvā svasute apy āha — aham iva yuvām api mithunam utpādayatam
          iti/ tataḥ kālarātrir mahādevaṃ puruṣaṃ svarāṃ striyaṃ ca janayām āsa/ sarasvatī ca viṣṇuṃ
          puruṣaṃ gaurīṃ ca striyam udapādayat/ tataś cādir vivāham akarod akārayac ca/ evaṃ
          brahmaṇe svarāṃ viṣṇave śriyaṃ śivāya gaurīṃ dattvā śaktiyuktānāṃ teṣāṃ
          sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārākhyāni karmāṇi pratyapādayad iti/ tad etanmataṃ

          pramātṛtvādiprapañca ity alam atiprasaṅgena/

 nanu kimarthaṃ pramātṛtvādīnām āvidyakatvaṃ nigadyate/ brahmajñānena nivartanāya jīvasya

 setuṃ dṛṣṭvā vimucyeta brahmahā brahmahatyayā/ 
 
 ityādinā pāpaṃ sanīsrasyate/ viṣayadoṣadarśanena rāgo dandahyate/ tārkṣyadhyānena viṣaṃ

 [l. 16.805] 
 
 lokāvagatasāmarthyaḥ śabdo vede ’pi bodhakaḥ/ 
 
 it nyāyena lokāvalokitāṃ padaśaktiṃ padārthayogyatāṃ corarīkṛtya pracaratīti/ aparathā

 apūrvāṅgīkaraṇānupapatteś ° ] ASS;  apūrvāṅgīkaraṇānupapattiś ° A. 
  ca/ loke ca śuktivyaktitattvābhivyaktāv apanīyamānasyāropitasya mithyātvadṛṣṭau
          taddṛṣṭāntāvaṣṭambhenātmatattvasākṣātkāravidyāpanodyasyāvidyakasya bandhasya
          mithyātvānumānasaṃbhavāt/ vimataṃ mithyā adhiṣṭhānatattvajñānanivartyatvāc
          chuktikārūpyavad iti/ na ca vimataṃ satyaṃ bhāsamānatvād iti pratiprayoge samānabalatayā
          bādhapratirodhaḥ/ pratirodhabhiyānyataradoṣatvasaṃbhavād iti vaditavyam/
          marumarīcikodakādau savyabhicārāt/ abādhitatvena viśeṣaṇān na doṣa iti cet — maivaṃ
          bhāṣiṣṭhāḥ/ viśeṣaṇāsiddheḥ/ 
 tatredaṃ bhavān pṛṣṭo vyācaṣṭām/ katipayapuruṣakatipayakālābādhitatvaṃ hetuviśeṣaṇaṃ
          kriyate sarvathā bādhavaidhuryaṃ vā/ na prathamaḥ/ 
 [l. 16.820] 
 
 yatnenānumito ’py arthaḥ kuśalair anumātṛbhiḥ/ 
 abhiyuktatarair anyair anyathaivopapādyate// 
 
 iti nyāyena tricaturapratipattṛpratipāditasyāpi pratipattrantareṇa prakārāntaram
          urarīkṛtya pratipādanāt/ nāpi caramaḥ/ sarvathā bādhavaidhuryasyāsarvajñadurjñeyatvāt/
          yady evaṃ hanta tarhi jñānātmano ’pi satyatvaṃ nāvagamyata iti cet — maivaṃ maṃsthāḥ/ tat
          satyaṃ sa ātmā ity āgamasaṃvādagateḥ/ na ca prapañce ’py ayaṃ nyāya iti mantavyam/
          tādṛśasyāgamasyānupalambhāt/ pratyutādvitīyatvaṃ śrāvayantyāḥ śruteḥ prapañcamithyātva eva
          pakṣapātāt/ nanu kalpanāmātraśarīrasya pakṣasapakṣavipakṣādeḥ sarvasulabhatvena
          jayaparājayavyavasthayā kathaṃ kathā pratheta/ kātra kathaṃtā/ 
 [l. 16.831] 
 evaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥ iti nyāyena tricaturakakṣyāviśrāntasya
          tattadābhāsalakṣaṇānāliṅgitasya dūṣaṇabhūṣaṇādes tatra kathāṅgatvāṅgīkārāt/ ata evoktaṃ
          khaṇḍanakāreṇa — vyāvahārikīṃ pramāṇasattām ādāya vicārārambhaḥ iti/ na ca bhedagrāhibhiḥ
          pramāṇair advaitaśruter jaghanyateti śaṅkyam/ brahmaṇi pāramārthikasatyatvena
          tadāvedikāyās tattvāvedanalakṣaṇaprāmāṇyāyāḥ śruter vyāvahārikapramāṇabhāvānāṃ
          pratyakṣādīnāṃ ca vibhinnaviṣayatayā parasparaṃ bādhyabādhakabhāvāsaṃbhavāt/ tad apy uktaṃ
          tenaiva — 
 
 tadadvaitaśrutes tāvad bādhaḥ pratyakṣataḥ kṣataḥ/ 
 nānumānādi taṃ kartuṃ tavāpi kṣamate mate// 
 dhīdhanā bādhanāyāsyās tadā prajñāṃ prayacchatha/ 
 kṣeptuṃ cintāmaṇiṃ pāṇilabdham abdhau yadīcchatha// 
 
 tasmāt tattvajñānena nivartanāyāsya bandhasyājñānakalpitatvam aṅgīkartavyam/ yata uktaṃ
          yato jñānam ajñānasya nivartakam iti/ 
 [l. 16.846] 
 yad uktaṃ satyasyāpi duritasya setudarśanena nivṛttir upalabhyata iti/ tad ayuktam/
          vihitakriyānuṣṭhānena janitasya dharmasyādharmanivartakatvadhrauvyāt/ dharmeṇa pāpam
          apanudanti iti śruteḥ/ pramāṇavastuparatantraśālinyā darśanakriyāyāś
          coditapuruṣaprayatnatantratvābhāvena vidhānāsaṃbhavāt/ 
 
 brahmahatyām pramucyeta tasmin snātvā mahodadhau/ 
 
 ityādismṛtivihitabrahmacaryāṅgasahitadūrataradeśagamanasādhyabrahma-hanananivṛttiphalakasetusnānapraśaṃsārthatvāt/
          yasya hi darśanamātreṇaiva duritopaśamaḥ kim uta snānena/ anyathā dūragamanānarthakyaṃ
          prasajjeta/ tatra kharādīnām apy anarthanivṛttir āpatet/ andhasya na syāc ca/ 
 nanu — 
 
 agnicit kapilā rājā satī bhikṣur mahodadhiḥ/ 
 dṛṣṭamātrāḥ punanty ete tasmāt paśyeta nityaśaḥ// 
 
 iti kvacid darśanakriyāyā api vidhānaṃ darīdṛśyata iti cet — 
 maivaṃ vocaḥ/ tatrāpy anayaivānupapattyāgnicidādyarghaparicaryādāv eva
          tātparyāvadhāraṇāt/ yac coktaṃ viṣayadoṣadarśanād rāgo dandahyata iti/ tatra
          viṣayadoṣadarśanena virodhabhūtānabhiratisaṃjñakavairāgyaikaprādurbhāvād rāganivṛttau
          tadadarśanamātram iti na vyabhicāraḥ/ yad api tārkṣyadhyānādinā viṣādi satyaṃ vinaśyatīti/
          tan na śliṣyate/ tatrāpi mantraprayogādikriyāyā eva viṣādyapanodakatvāt/ dhyānasya
          pramātvābhāvāc ca/ yad avādy aupādhikasya jīvabhāvasyopādhinivṛttyā nivṛttau
          brahmabhāvopapatter na tadartham arthavaitathyakathanam iti/ tad api
          kāśakuśāvalambanakalpam/ vikalpāsahatvāt/ kim upādheḥ satyatvam abhipretya mithyātvaṃ vā/
          na prathamaḥ/ pramāṇābhāvāt/ nāparaḥ/ iṣṭāpatteḥ/ tasmād āvidyako bheda iti śrutāv
          advitīyatvopapattaye ’bhidhīyate na tu vyasanitayā/ 
 [l. 16.871] 
 yadi vastutaḥ sarvopadravarahitam ātmatattvaṃ tarhi kathaṃkāraṃ dehādirūpaṃ kārāgāraṃ
          kāraṃkāraṃ punaḥ punas tatra praviśati/ tad atiphalgu/ avidyāyā anāditvena dattottaratvāt/
          ato nivṛttyupāya evānveṣaṇīyaḥ prekṣāvatā/ na tu vismayaḥ kartavyaḥ/ tataś ca
          tattvamasādividyayā tadavidyānivṛttau niratiśayānandātmalābharūpaparamapuruṣārthaḥ
          setsyati/ tathā cāpastambasmṛtiḥ — ātmalābhān na paraṃ vidyata iti/ 
 nanv asau nityalabdhaḥ/ na hi svayam eva svasyālabdho bhavati/ 
 satyam/ kiṃ tv anādimāyāsaṃbandhāt kṣīrodakavat samudācāravṛttitāṃ na labhate/ tathā ca
          yathā śabarādibhir bālyāt svasutaiḥ saha vardhito rājaputras tajjātīyam ātmānam avagacchan
          bandhubhir ya evaṃbhūto rājā sa tvam asīti bodhite svarūpe labdhasvarūpa iva bhavati tathā
          veśyāsthānīyayānādyavidyayā svabhāvāntaraṃ nīta ātmā mātṛsthānīyayā tat tvam asītyādikayā
          śrutyā svabhāvaṃ nīyate/ etad āhus traividyavṛddhāḥ — 
 [l. 16.884] 
 
 nīcānāṃ vasatau tadīyatanayaiḥ sārdhaṃ ciraṃ vardhitas 
 tajjātīyam avaiti rājatanayaḥ svātmānam apy añjasā/ 
 saṃvāde mahadādibhiḥ saha vasaṃs tadvad bhavet pūruṣaḥ 
 svātmānaṃ sukhaduḥkhajālakalitaṃ mithyaiva dhiṅ manyate// 
 dātā bhogaparaḥ samagravibhavo yaḥ śāsitā duṣkṛtām 
 rājā sa tvam asīti rakṣitṛmukhāc chrutvā yathāvat sa tu/ 
 rājībhūya jayārtham eva yatate tadvat pumān bodhitaḥ/ 
 śrutyā tat tvam asīty apāsya duritaṃ brahmaiva saṃpadyate// 
 
 etenaitat pratyuktaṃ yad uktaṃ paraiḥ kiṃ dvayos tādātmyam ekasya vā/ nādyaḥ/
          advaitabhaṅgaprasaṅgāt/ na dvitīyaḥ/ asaṃbhavād iti/ 
 tan na/ avidyāparikalpitabhedanivṛttiparatvena tat tvam
          asyāditādātmyavādaprāmāṇyopapatteḥ/ tau ca paryanuyogaparihārāv agrāhiṣātāṃ
          manīṣibhiḥ/ 
 [l. 16.896] 
 
 na dvayor asti tādātmyaṃ na caikasyādvayatvataḥ/ 
 aprāmāṇyaṃ śruter evaṃ nāropadhvaṃsamātrataḥ// iti 
 
 tataś ca tat tvam asīti tattvaṃpadārthaśravaṇamananabhāvanābalabhuvā
          sākṣātkāreṇānādyavidyānivṛttau saccidānandaikarasabrahmāvirbhāvaḥ saṃpatsyata iti brahmaṇo
          jijñāsyatvaṃ prathamasūtroktaṃ yuktam/ 
 [l. 16.901] 
 
 ajñātaṃ viṣayo brahma jñātaṃ tac ca prayojanam/ 
 mumukṣur adhikārī syāt saṃbandhaḥ śaktitaḥ sruteḥ// iti/ 
 
 janmādy asya yataḥ iti dvitīyasūtre brahma svarūpalakṣaṇataṭasthalakṣaṇābhyāṃ nyarūpi/
          tatra svarūpāntargatatve sati vyāvartakaṃ svarūpalakṣaṇaṃ satyaṃ jñānam anantaṃ brahma
          ityādivedāntaiḥ pratipāditam/ tasya satyajñānādyātmakasvarūpāntargatatve sati
          vyāvartakatvāt/ taṭasthalakṣaṇaṃ yato vā imāni ityādīni vākyāni nirūpayanti
          jagajjanmādikāraṇatvena/ tad uktaṃ vivaraṇe — 
 
 jagajjanmasthitidhvaṃsā yataḥ sidhyanti kāraṇāt/ 
 tat svarūpataṭasthābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyāṃ pradarśyate// iti/ 
 
 [l. 16.912] 
 śāstrayonitvāt iti tṛtīyasūtre prathamavarṇakena ṣaṣṭhīsamāsam āśritya sarvajñatvaṃ
          pratyapādi/ dvitīyavarṇakena bahuvrīhisamāsam abhyupagamya brahmaṇo vedāntapramāṇakatvaṃ
          pratyajñāyi/ 
 [l. 16.915] 
 tat tu samanvayāt iti caturthe sūtre prathamavarṇakena vedāntānāṃ brahmaṇi tātparyaṃ
          pratyapādi/ dvitīyavarṇakena vedāntānāṃ pratipattividhiśeṣatayā brahmapratipādakatvaṃ
          pratyakṣe 'pi/ diṅmātram atra pradarśitam/ śiṣṭaṃ śāstra eva spaṣṭam iti sakalaṃ
          samañjasam// 
 śrīr astu// 
 [l. 16.920] 
 iti sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe sakaladarśanaśirolaṃkāraratnaṃ śrīmacchāṃkaradarśanaṃ
          samāptam// 
 samāpto ’yam sarvadarśanasaṃgrahaḥ//
